## 22:1-2 — verses 1-2 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Exegesis of Surat al-Hajj

[It is Meccan]

In the name of Allah, the Most Gracious, the Most Merciful.

The Exalted speaks, commanding His servants to fear Him, and informing them of what they will encounter of the terrors of the Day of Resurrection, its tremors and its conditions. The commentators have differed concerning the tremor of the Hour: is it after the people rise from their graves on the Day of their resurrection, into the assembly grounds of the Resurrection? Or is that an expression referring to the tremor of the earth before the people rise from their graves? As the Exalted said: {When the earth is shaken with its violent shaking, and the earth discharges its burdens} [al-Zalzalah: 1, 2], and the Exalted said: {And the earth and the mountains are lifted up and crushed with a single crushing blow, then on that day the Occurrence will occur} [al-Haqqah: 14, 15], and the Exalted said: {When the earth is shaken with a violent shaking, and the mountains are crumbled with a crumbling, and become scattered dust} [al-Waqi'ah: 4-6].

Some said: this tremor occurs at the end of the life of this world, at the beginning of the conditions of the Hour.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] Alqamah, concerning His saying: {Indeed the tremor of the Hour is a mighty thing}, said: before the Hour.

Ibn Abi Hatim also related it from the hadith of al-Thawri, from Mansur and al-A'mash, from Ibrahim, from Alqamah, mentioning it. He said: something similar was related from al-Sha'bi, Ibrahim, and Ubayd ibn Umayr.

Abu Kudaynah said, from Ata', from Amir al-Sha'bi, concerning {O mankind, fear your Lord} the verse: he said, this is in this world, before the Day of Resurrection.

The Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir presented the basis of those who held this view in the hadith of the Horn (al-Sur), by the route of Isma'il ibn Rafi', judge of the people of Medina, from Yazid ibn Abi Ziyad, from a man of the Ansar, from Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, from a man, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When Allah finished creating the heavens and the earth, He created the Horn, and gave it to Israfil, who holds it to his mouth, gazing steadily toward the Throne, awaiting when he will be commanded." Abu Hurayrah said: O Messenger of Allah, what is the Horn?

He said: "A horn." He said: what is it like? He said: "A mighty horn, blown three times: the first is the Blast of Terror, the second is the Blast of Swooning, and the third is the Blast of Rising to stand before the Lord of the Worlds. Allah commands Israfil with the first blast, saying: Blow the Blast of Terror. So the people of the heavens and the people of the earth are terrified, except whom Allah wills, and He commands him to prolong and extend it without pause. This is what Allah, the Exalted, refers to when He says: {And these await nothing but a single Blast, from which there will be no delay} [Sad: 15]. Then Allah moves the mountains, and they become like a mirage, and the earth is shaken violently with its inhabitants, and this is what Allah, the Exalted, refers to when He says: {The Day when the Quaking One quakes, followed by the Subsequent One, hearts on that day trembling} [al-Nazi'at: 6-8]. The earth becomes like a ship foundering in the sea, buffeted by waves that overturn it with its inhabitants, and like a lantern hanging from the Throne, swayed by the winds.

The people stretch out upon its surface, nursing mothers become oblivious, pregnant women give birth, children turn grey-haired, and the devils fly off in flight until they reach the far horizons, where the angels meet them and strike their faces, and they turn back, and the people flee, calling out to one another. This is what Allah, the Exalted, refers to when He says: {The Day of mutual calling, the Day when you will turn your backs fleeing, you will have no protector from Allah, and whomever Allah leads astray has no guide} [Ghafir: 32, 33]. While they are in this state, the earth splits from one edge to the other, and they see a tremendous thing, and such distress seizes them as only Allah knows. Then they look up at the sky, and it is like molten metal, then its sun is eclipsed and its moon is eclipsed, its stars are scattered, and then it is stripped away from them." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "And the dead know nothing of any of this." Abu Hurayrah said: who then are those Allah excepted, when He says: {So all who are in the heavens and all who are in the earth will be terrified, except whom Allah wills} [al-Naml: 87]? He said: those are the martyrs, for terror only reaches the living, and those are alive with their Lord, provided for, and Allah has protected them from the evil of that day and given them safety. It is the punishment of Allah which He sends upon the worst of His creation. This is what Allah says: {O mankind, fear your Lord, indeed the tremor of the Hour is a mighty thing. On the day you see it, every nursing mother will be oblivious to what she nursed, and every pregnant woman will deliver her burden, and you will see mankind as if drunk, though they are not drunk, but the punishment of Allah is severe}.

This hadith was related by al-Tabarani, Ibn Jarir, Ibn Abi Hatim, and more than one other, at great length.

The purpose it serves is to indicate that this tremor occurs before the Day of the Hour, and it was attributed to the Hour because of its proximity to it, just as one says "the signs of the Hour," and the like. And Allah knows best.

Others said: rather, this terror, tremor, and turmoil occurs on the Day of Resurrection in the assembly grounds, after the rising from the graves. Ibn Jarir preferred this view. They cited hadiths in support:

The first: Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Imran ibn Husayn, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, while on one of his journeys, when the pace of travel among his companions had become uneven, he raised his voice with these two verses: {O mankind, fear your Lord, indeed the tremor of the Hour is a mighty thing. On the day you see it, every nursing mother will be oblivious to what she nursed, and every pregnant woman will deliver her burden, and you will see mankind as if drunk, though they are not drunk, but the punishment of Allah is severe}.

When his companions heard this, they urged their mounts forward, knowing that he was about to say something. When they had gathered closely around him, he said: "Do you know what day that is? It is the day when Adam, peace be upon him, will be called, and his Lord, Mighty and Majestic, will call to him and say: O Adam, send forth your delegation to the Fire. He will say: O Lord, and what is the delegation to the Fire? He will say: Out of every thousand, nine hundred and ninety-nine to the Fire, and one to the Garden." He said: his companions were struck with dismay, so that not one of them showed a smiling face. When he saw that, he said: "Rejoice and act righteously, for by the One in whose hand is the soul of Muhammad, you are accompanied by two created kinds that have never accompanied anything without outnumbering it: Gog and Magog, and those of the children of Adam and the children of Iblis who have perished." He said: so their distress was relieved, then he said: "Act righteously and rejoice, for by the One in whose hand is the soul of Muhammad, you are among mankind only like a mole on the flank of a camel, or a marking on the foreleg of a beast."

This was likewise related by al-Tirmidhi and al-Nasa'i in the Book of Exegesis of their respective Sunan works, from Muhammad ibn Bashshar, from Yahya (who is al-Qattan), from Hisham (who is al-Dastuwa'i), from Qatadah, with similar wording. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan sahih (sound and authentic).

Another route for this hadith: al-Tirmidhi said: [chain] from Imran ibn Husayn, that the Prophet ﷺ said, when {O mankind, fear your Lord, indeed the tremor of the Hour is a mighty thing} was revealed, up to His saying {but the punishment of Allah is severe}, this was revealed to him while he was on a journey, and he said: "Do you know what day that is?" They said: Allah and His Messenger know best. He said: "That is a day when Allah will say to Adam: send forth the delegation of the Fire. He will say: O Lord, and what is the delegation of the Fire? He will say: nine hundred and ninety-nine to the Fire, and one to the Garden." The Muslims then began to weep, so the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Draw near and be steadfast, for there has never been a prophethood except that a period of ignorance (jahiliyyah) preceded it." He said: "The number will be taken from the people of ignorance, and if it is not complete, it will be completed from the hypocrites. Your likeness compared to the other nations is only like the marking on the foreleg of a beast, or the mole on the flank of a camel." Then he said: "Indeed I hope that you will be a quarter of the people of the Garden." So they exclaimed in praise (takbir). Then he said: "Indeed I hope that you will be a third of the people of the Garden." So they exclaimed in praise. Then he said: "Indeed I hope that you will be half of the people of the Garden." So they exclaimed in praise. He said: and I do not know whether he also said "two thirds" or not.

This was likewise related by Imam Ahmad from Sufyan ibn Uyaynah. Then al-Tirmidhi also said: this is a hasan sahih hadith.

It was also related from Sa'id ibn Abi Arubah, from al-Hasan, from Imran ibn al-Husayn. Ibn Abi Hatim related it from the hadith of Sa'id ibn Abi Arubah, from Qatadah, from al-Hasan and al-Ala' ibn Ziyad al-Adawi, from Imran ibn al-Husayn, mentioning it.

Likewise, Ibn Jarir narrated from Bundar, from Ghundar, from Awf, from al-Hasan, who said: it reached me that when the Messenger of Allah ﷺ returned from the Battle of al-Usrah and his companions were with him, after he had drawn near to Medina, he recited: {O mankind, fear your Lord. Indeed, the shaking of the Hour is a tremendous thing.} And he mentioned the hadith, giving an account similar to that of Ibn Jud'an. And Allah knows best.

The second hadith: Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father narrated to us, Ibn al-Tabba' narrated to us, Abu Sufyan (meaning al-Ma'mari) narrated to us, from Ma'mar, from Qatadah, from Anas, who said: {Indeed, the shaking of the Hour is a tremendous thing} was revealed. And he mentioned an account similar to that of al-Hasan from Imran, except that he said: "and those who perish among the disbelieving jinn and men."

Ibn Jarir narrated it in full, from the hadith of Ma'mar.

The third hadith: Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father narrated to us, Sa'id ibn Sulayman narrated to us, Abbad (meaning ibn al-Awwam) narrated to us, Hilal ibn Khabbab narrated to us, from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ recited this verse. And he mentioned an account similar to it, and in it he said: "I truly hope that you will be a quarter of the people of Paradise," then he said: "I truly hope that you will be a third of the people of Paradise," then he said: "I truly hope that you will be half of the people of Paradise," and they rejoiced. He also added: "and you are but one part out of a thousand parts."

The fourth hadith: al-Bukhari said regarding this verse: Umar ibn Hafs narrated to us, my father narrated to us, al-A'mash narrated to us, Abu Salih narrated to us, from Abu Sa'id, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah, Exalted is He, will say on the Day of Resurrection: O Adam! He will say: here I am at Your service, and at Your pleasure, my Lord. Then a voice will call out: indeed Allah commands you to bring forth from your progeny a company for the Fire. He will say: O my Lord, what is the company for the Fire? He will say: out of every thousand, I think he said, nine hundred and ninety-nine." He said: "It is then that every pregnant woman will drop her load, and every child will turn grey-haired. {And you will see mankind as if intoxicated, but they are not intoxicated. Rather, the punishment of Allah is severe.}" That was hard on the people until their faces changed. The Prophet ﷺ said: "nine hundred and ninety-nine from Gog and Magog, and one from you. Then you will be, among mankind, like a black hair on the flank of a white ox, or like a white hair on the flank of a black ox. And I truly hope that you will be a quarter of the people of Paradise." So we said "Allahu akbar." Then he said: "a third of the people of Paradise." So we said "Allahu akbar." Then he said: "half of the people of Paradise." So we said "Allahu akbar."

Al-Bukhari also narrated it in another place, as did Muslim, and al-Nasa'i in his Tafsir, through various chains, from al-A'mash, with this wording.

The fifth hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Ammar ibn Muhammad (the nephew of Sufyan al-Thawri) and Ubaydah narrated to us, the meaning being the same, both from Ibrahim ibn Muslim, from Abu al-Ahwas, from Abdullah, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed, Allah will send forth on the Day of Resurrection a caller who will call out: O Adam! Indeed, Allah commands you to send forth from your progeny a company for the Fire. Adam will say: O my Lord, who are they? It will be said to him: out of every hundred, ninety-nine." A man among the people said: who then is the one who will be saved among us after this, O Messenger of Allah? He said: "Do you know that you are, among mankind, nothing but like the mole on the chest of a camel."

Imam Ahmad narrated this alone with this chain and this wording.

The sixth hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Yahya narrated to us, from Hatim ibn Abi Saghirah, Ibn Abi Mulaykah narrated to us, that al-Qasim ibn Muhammad informed him, from Aishah, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "You will be gathered on the Day of Resurrection barefoot, naked, and uncircumcised." Aishah said: O Messenger of Allah, will men and women look at one another? He said: "O Aishah, the matter is too severe for that to concern them."

Both al-Bukhari and Muslim narrated it in their Sahihs.

The seventh hadith: Imam Ahmad said: Yahya ibn Ishaq narrated to us, Ibn Lahi'ah narrated to us, from Khalid ibn Abi Imran, from al-Qasim ibn Muhammad, from Aishah, who said: I said: O Messenger of Allah, will a loved one remember his loved one on the Day of Resurrection? He said: "O Aishah, at three moments, no. At the Scales, until it becomes heavy or light, no. And when the records fly about, whether one is given his in his right hand or his left, no. And when a neck comes forth from the Fire and coils around them, raging against them, and that neck says: I have been charged with three, I have been charged with three, I have been charged with three: I have been charged with whoever claimed another god along with Allah, and I have been charged with whoever does not believe in the Day of Reckoning, and I have been charged with every obstinate tyrant." He said: "So it coils around them and throws them into overwhelming depths. And Hell has a bridge finer than a hair and sharper than a sword, upon it are hooks and thorns that seize whomever Allah wills, while people cross over it like the blink of an eye, like lightning, like the wind, like the finest of horses and riding beasts. And the angels say: My Lord, grant safety, grant safety. So there is one saved unharmed, one saved but scratched, and one rolled over onto his face into the Fire."

The hadiths and reports about the terrors of the Day of Resurrection are very numerous, and have another place for discussion. This is why Allah, Exalted is He, said: {Indeed, the shaking of the Hour is a tremendous thing}, meaning: a great matter, a momentous affair, a horrifying visitation, a terrifying event, and an astonishing occurrence.

The shaking (al-zilzal) is what befalls souls of terror and fright, as Allah, Exalted is He, said: {There the believers were tried and shaken with a severe shaking} [al-Ahzab: 11].

Then Allah, Exalted is He, said: {The Day you see it}: this is from the category of the pronoun of the matter (damir al-sha'n, an anticipatory pronoun referring to something explained afterward). This is why He said, explaining it: {every nursing mother will be distracted from that which she nursed}, meaning: she will be so preoccupied by the terror of what she sees that she will be diverted from the one most beloved to her, the one for whom she has the greatest tenderness of all people. She will be stunned away from him even while in the state of nursing him. This is why He said {every nursing mother} (kullu murdi'atin) and did not say "murdi'in" (nursing, without the feminine emphatic form), and He said {from that which she nursed}, meaning: from her nursing infant before his weaning.

And His saying: {and every pregnant one will deliver her load}, meaning: before its completion, due to the severity of the terror. {And you will see mankind as if intoxicated} and it was also recited "sakra" (a variant reading), meaning: from the severity of the matter in which they find themselves, their minds having become stunned and their intellects vanished, so that whoever sees them supposes them to be intoxicated. {But they are not intoxicated. Rather, the punishment of Allah is severe.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

تَفْسِيرُ سُورَةِ الْحَجِّ

[وَهِيَ مَكِّيَّةٌ] .

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَنِ الرَّحِيمِ

* *

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى آمِرًا عِبَادَهُ بِتَقْوَاهُ، وَمُخْبِرًا لَهُمْ بِمَا يُسْتَقْبَلُونَ مِنْ أَهْوَالِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَزَلَازِلِهَا وَأَحْوَالِهِا. وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ الْمُفَسِّرُونَ فِي زَلْزَلَةِ السَّاعَةِ: هَلْ هِيَ بَعْدَ قِيَامِ النَّاسِ مِنْ قُبُورِهِمْ يَوْمَ نَشُورِهِمْ إِلَى عَرصَات الْقِيَامَةِ؟ أَوْ ذَلِكَ عِبَارَةٌ عَنْ زَلْزَلَةِ الْأَرْضِ قَبْلَ قِيَامِ النَّاسِ مَنْ أَجْدَاثِهِمْ؟ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِذَا زُلْزِلَتِ الأرْضُ زِلْزَالَهَا. وَأَخْرَجَتِ الأرْضُ أَثْقَالَهَا﴾ [الزَّلْزَلَةِ: ١، ٢] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَحُمِلَتِ الأرْضُ وَالْجِبَالُ فَدُكَّتَا دَكَّةً * وَاحِدَةً فَيَوْمَئِذٍ وَقَعَتِ الْوَاقِعَةُ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١٤، ١٥] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِذَا رُجَّتِ الأرْضُ رَجًّا. وَبُسَّتِ الْجِبَالُ بَسًّا. فَكَانَتْ هَبَاءً مُنْبَثًّا﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٤ -٦] .

فَقَالَ قَائِلُونَ: هَذِهِ الزَّلْزَلَةُ كَائِنَةٌ فِي آخِرِ عُمُرِ الدُّنْيَا، وَأَوَّلِ أَحْوَالِ السَّاعَةِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ بَشَّار، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عَلْقَمَة فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ ، قَالَ: قَبْلَ السَّاعَةِ.

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ وَالْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ عَلْقَمَةَ، فَذَكَرَهُ. قَالَ: وَرُوِيَ عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمَ، وعُبَيْد بْنِ عُمَيْر، نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو كُدَيْنَةَ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ عَامِرٍ الشَّعْبِيِّ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: هَذَا فِي الدُّنْيَا قَبْلَ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَقَدْ أَوْرَدَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ بن جَرِيرٍ مُسْتَنَدَ مَنْ قَالَ ذَلِكَ فِي حَدِيثِ الصُّور، من رواية إسماعيل ابن رَافِعٍ قَاضِي أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي زِيَادٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيِّ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمَّا فَرَغَ مِنْ خَلْقِ السَّمَوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ خَلَقَ الصُّور، فَأَعْطَاهُ إِسْرَافِيلَ، فَهُوَ وَاضِعُهُ عَلَى فِيه، شَاخِصٌ بِبَصَرِهِ إِلَى العَرش، يَنْتَظِرُ مَتَى يُؤْمَرُ". قَالَ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَمَا الصُّورُ؟

قَالَ: "قَرْنٌ" قَالَ: فَكَيْفَ هُوَ؟ قَالَ: "قَرْنٌ عَظِيمٌ يُنْفَخُ فِيهِ ثَلَاثُ نفخات، الأولى نفخة الفزع، وَالثَّانِيَةُ نَفْخَةُ الصَّعْق، وَالثَّالِثَةُ نَفْخَةُ الْقِيَامِ لِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ، يَأْمُرُ اللَّهُ إِسْرَافِيلَ بِالنَّفْخَةِ الْأُولَى فَيَقُولُ: انفخ نَفْخَةَ الْفَزَعِ. فيفزعُ أَهْلُ السَّمَوَاتِ وَأَهْلُ الْأَرْضِ، إِلَّا مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ، وَيَأْمُرُهُ فَيَمُدُّهَا وَيُطَوِّلُهَا وَلَا يَفْتُرُ، وَهِيَ الَّتِي يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا يَنْظُرُ هَؤُلاءِ إِلا صَيْحَةً وَاحِدَةً مَا لَهَا مِنْ فَوَاقٍ﴾ [ص: ١٥] فَيُسير اللَّهُ الْجِبَالَ، فَتَكُونُ سَرَابًا وتُرج الْأَرْضُ بِأَهْلِهَا رَجًّا، وَهِيَ الَّتِي يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تَرْجُفُ الرَّاجِفَةُ. تَتْبَعُهَا الرَّادِفَةُ. قُلُوبٌ يَوْمَئِذٍ وَاجِفَةٌ﴾ [النَّازِعَاتِ: ٦ -٨] ، فَتَكُونُ الْأَرْضُ، كَالسَّفِينَةِ الْمُوبِقَةِ فِي الْبَحْرِ، تَضْرِبُهَا الْأَمْوَاجُ تَكْفَؤُهَا بِأَهْلِهَا، وَكَالْقِنْدِيلِ الْمُعَلَّقِ بِالْعَرْشِ تُرَجِّحُهُ الْأَرْوَاحُ.

فَيَمْتَدُّ النَّاسُ عَلَى ظَهْرِهَا، فَتَذْهَلُ الْمَرَاضِعُ، وَتَضَعُ الْحَوَامِلُ. وَيَشِيبُ الْوِلْدَانُ، وَتَطِيرُ الشَّيَاطِينُ هَارِبَةً، حَتَّى تَأْتِيَ الْأَقْطَارَ، فَتَلَقَّاهَا الْمَلَائِكَةُ فَتَضْرِبُ وُجُوهَهَا، فَتَرْجِعُ، وَيُوَلِّي النَّاسُ مُدْبِرِينَ، يُنَادِي بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا، وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ التَّنَادِ * يَوْمَ تُوَلُّونَ مُدْبِرِينَ مَا لَكُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ مِنْ عَاصِمٍ وَمَنْ يُضْلِلِ اللَّهُ فَمَا لَهُ مِنْ هَادٍ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ٣٢، ٣٣] فَبَيْنَمَا هُمْ عَلَى ذَلِكَ إِذِ انْصَدَعَتِ الْأَرْضُ مِنْ قُطْرٍ إِلَى قُطْرٍ، فَرَأوا أَمْرًا عَظِيمًا، فَأَخَذَهُمْ لِذَلِكَ مِنَ الْكَرْبِ مَا اللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِهِ، ثُمَّ نَظَرُوا إِلَى السَّمَاءِ فَإِذَا هِيَ كَالْمُهْلِ، ثُمَّ خُسِفَ شَمْسُهَا وخُسفَ قَمَرُهَا، وَانْتَثَرَتْ نُجُومُهَا، ثُمَّ كُشِطت عَنْهُمْ" قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَالْأَمْوَاتُ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ ذَلِكَ" قَالَ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: فَمَنِ اسْتَثْنَى اللَّهُ حِينَ يَقُولُ: ﴿فَفَزِعَ مَنْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَنْ فِي الأرْضِ إِلا مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ﴾ [النَّمْلِ: ٨٧] ؟ قَالَ: أُولَئِكَ الشُّهَدَاءُ، وَإِنَّمَا يَصِلُ الْفَزَعُ إِلَى الْأَحْيَاءِ، أُولَئِكَ أَحْيَاءٌ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ يُرْزَقُونَ، وَقَاهُمُ اللَّهُ شَرَّ ذَلِكَ الْيَوْمِ وَآمَنَهُمْ، وَهُوَ عَذَابُ اللَّهِ يَبْعَثُهُ عَلَى شِرَارِ خَلْقِهِ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمْ إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ * يَوْمَ تَرَوْنَهَا تَذْهَلُ كُلُّ مُرْضِعَةٍ عَمَّا أَرْضَعَتْ وَتَضَعُ كُلُّ ذَاتِ حَمْلٍ حَمْلَهَا وَتَرَى النَّاسَ سُكَارَى وَمَا هُمْ بِسُكَارَى وَلَكِنَّ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ شَدِيدٌ﴾ .

وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ قَدْ رَوَاهُ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مُطَوَّلًا جِدًّا.

وَالْغَرَضُ مِنْهُ أَنَّهُ دَلَّ عَلَى أَنَّ هَذِهِ الزَّلْزَلَةَ كَائِنَةٌ قَبْلَ يَوْمِ السَّاعَةِ، وَأُضِيفَتْ إِلَى السَّاعَةِ لِقُرْبِهَا مِنْهَا، كَمَا يُقَالُ: أَشْرَاطُ السَّاعَةِ، وَنَحْوُ ذَلِكَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلْ ذَلِكَ هَوْلٌ وَفَزَعٌ وَزِلْزَالٌ وَبِلْبَالٌ، كَائِنٌ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ فِي الْعَرَصَاتِ، بَعْدَ الْقِيَامَةِ مِنَ الْقُبُورِ. وَاخْتَارَ ذَلِكَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ. وَاحْتَجُّوا بِأَحَادِيثَ:

الْأَوَّلُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، حَدَّثَنَا قَتَادَةُ، عن الحسن، عن عمران [ابن] حُصَين؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ وَهُوَ فِي بَعْضِ أَسْفَارِهِ، وَقَدْ تَفَاوَتَ بَيْنَ أَصْحَابِهِ السَّيْرُ، رَفَعَ بِهَاتَيْنِ الْآيَتَيْنِ صَوْتَهُ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمْ إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ يَوْمَ تَرَوْنَهَا تَذْهَلُ كُلُّ مُرْضِعَةٍ عَمَّا أَرْضَعَتْ وَتَضَعُ كُلُّ ذَاتِ حَمْلٍ حَمْلَهَا وَتَرَى النَّاسَ سُكَارَى وَمَا هُمْ بِسُكَارَى وَلَكِنَّ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ شَدِيدٌ﴾

فَلَمَّا سَمِعَ أَصْحَابُهُ بِذَلِكَ حَثْوا المُطي، وَعَرَفُوا أَنَّهُ عِنْدَ قَوْلٍ يَقُولُهُ، فَلَمَّا تَأَشَّهُوا حَوْلَهُ قَالَ: " أَتَدْرُونَ أَيُّ يَوْمٍ ذَاكَ؟ يَوْمَ يُنَادَى آدَمُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، فَيُنَادِيهِ رَبُّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، فَيَقُولُ: يَا آدَمُ، ابْعَثْ بَعْثَكَ إِلَى النَّارِ فَيَقُولُ: يَا رَبِّ، وَمَا بَعْثُ النَّارِ؟ فَيَقُولُ: مِنْ كُلِّ أَلْفٍ تِسْعُمِائَةٍ وَتِسْعَةٌ وَتِسْعُونَ فِي النَّارِ، وَوَاحِدٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ". قَالَ فَأَبْلَسَ أَصْحَابُهُ حَتَّى مَا أَوْضَحُوا بِضَاحِكَةٍ، فَلَمَّا رَأَى ذَلِكَ قَالَ: "أَبْشِرُوا وَاعْمَلُوا، فَوَالَّذِي نَفْسُ مُحَمَّدٍ بِيَدِهِ، إِنَّكُمْ لَمَعَ خَليقتين مَا كَانَتَا مَعَ شَيْءٍ قَطُّ إِلَّا كَثَّرَتَاهُ: يَأْجُوجُ وَمَأْجُوجُ، وَمَنْ هَلَكَ مِنْ بَنِي آدَمَ وَبَنِي إِبْلِيسَ" قَالَ: فسُرّي عَنْهُمْ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: اعْمَلُوا وَأَبْشِرُوا، فَوَالَّذِي نَفْسُ مُحَمَّدٍ بِيَدِهِ، مَا أَنْتُمْ فِي النَّاسِ إِلَّا كَالشَّامَةِ فِي جَنْبِ الْبَعِيرِ، أَوِ الرَّقْمَةِ فِي ذِرَاعِ الدَّابَّةِ".

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ وَالنَّسَائِيُّ فِي كِتَابِ التَّفْسِيرِ مِنْ سُنَنَيْهِمَا، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ بَشَّار، عَنْ يَحْيَى -وَهُوَ القَطَّان-عَنْ هِشَامٍ-وَهُوَ الدَّسْتُوَائِيُّ-عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، بِهِ بِنَحْوِهِ. وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

طَرِيقٌ أُخْرَى لِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ: قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ جُدعان، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ عِمْرَانِ بْنِ حُصَيْن؛ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمْ إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَكِنَّ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ شَدِيدٌ﴾ ، قَالَ: أُنْزِلَتْ عَلَيْهِ هَذِهِ، وَهُوَ فِي سَفَرٍ، فَقَالَ: "أَتَدْرُونَ أَيَّ يَوْمٍ ذَلِكَ؟ " فَقَالُوا: اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَعْلَمُ. قَالَ: "ذَلِكَ يَوْمٌ يَقُولُ اللَّهُ لِآدَمَ: ابْعَثْ بَعْثَ النَّارِ. قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، وَمَا بَعْثُ النَّارِ؟ قَالَ: تِسْعُمِائَةٌ وَتِسْعَةٌ وَتِسْعُونَ إِلَى النَّارِ، وَوَاحِدٌ إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ" فَأَنْشَأَ الْمُسْلِمُونَ يَبْكُونَ، فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "قَارِبُوا وسَدِّدوا، فَإِنَّهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ نُبُوَّةٌ قَطُّ إِلَّا كَانَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهَا جَاهِلِيَّةٌ" قَالَ: "فَيُؤْخَذُ الْعَدَدُ مِنَ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ، فَإِنْ تَمَّتْ وَإِلَّا كُمّلت مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، وَمَا مَثَلُكُمْ وَالْأُمَمُ إِلَّا كَمَثَلِ الرَّقمة فِي ذِرَاعِ الدَّابَّةِ، أَوْ كَالشَّامَةِ فِي جَنْبِ الْبَعِيرِ" ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا رُبْعَ أهل الجنة" فَكَبَّرُوا ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا ثُلُثَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ" فَكَبَّرُوا، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا نِصْفَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ" فَكَبَّرُوا، قَالَ: وَلَا أَدْرِي أَقَالَ الثُّلُثَيْنِ أَمْ لَا؟

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ ، ثُمَّ قَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ أَيْضًا: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ.

وَقَدْ رُوِيَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي عَرُوبة عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ عِمْرَانَ بْنِ الْحُصَيْنِ. وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَعِيدِ بْنِ أَبِي عَرُوبَةَ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ وَالْعَلَاءِ بْنِ زِيَادٍ الْعَدَوِيِّ، عَنْ عمران بن الحصين ، فذكره.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ بُنْدَار، عَنْ غُنْدَر، عَنْ عَوْفٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم لَمَّا قَفَلَ مِنْ غَزْوَةِ العُسرة وَمَعَهُ أَصْحَابُهُ بَعْدَ مَا شَارَفَ الْمَدِينَةَ قَرَأَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمْ إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ وَذَكَرَ الْحَدِيثَ ، فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَ سِيَاقِ ابْنِ جُدْعَان، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

الْحَدِيثُ الثَّانِي: قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ الطَبَّاع، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سُفْيَانَ -[يَعْنِي] الْمَعْمَرِيَّ-عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ أَنْسٍ قَالَ: نَزَلَتْ: ﴿إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ وَذَكَرَ -يَعْنِي: نَحْوَ سِيَاقِ الْحَسَنِ عَنْ عِمْرَانَ-غَيْرَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "وَمَنْ هَلَكَ مِنْ كَفَرَةِ الْجِنِّ وَالْإِنْسِ".

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ بِطُولِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَعْمَرٍ .

الْحَدِيثُ الثَّالِثُ: قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا سَعِيدُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبَّادٌ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ الْعَوَّامِ-حَدَّثَنَا هِلَالُ بْنُ خَبَّابٍ ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: تَلَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَهُ، وَقَالَ فِيهِ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا رُبُعَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ"، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا ثُلُثَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ" ثُمَّ قَالَ: "إِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا شَطْرَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ" فَفَرِحُوا، وَزَادَ أَيْضًا: "وَإِنَّمَا أَنْتُمْ جُزْءٌ مِنْ أَلْفِ جُزْءٍ" .

الْحَدِيثُ الرَّابِعُ: قَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ عِنْدَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ حَفْصٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو صَالِحٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ: يَا آدَمُ، فَيَقُولُ: لَبَّيْكَ رَبَّنَا وَسَعْدَيْكَ. فَيُنَادَى بِصَوْتٍ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَأْمُرُكَ أَنْ تُخْرِجَ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِكَ بَعْثًا إِلَى النَّارِ. قَالَ: يَا رَبِّ، وَمَا بَعْثُ النَّارِ؟ قَالَ: مِنْ كُلِّ أَلْفٍ -أَرَاهُ قَالَ-تِسْعَمِائَةٍ وَتِسْعَةً وَتِسْعِينَ . فَحِينَئِذٍ تَضَعُ الْحَامِلُ حَمْلَهَا، وَيَشِيبُ الْوَلِيدُ، ﴿وَتَرَى النَّاسَ سُكَارَى وَمَا هُمْ بِسُكَارَى وَلَكِنَّ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ شَدِيدٌ﴾ فَشَقَّ ذَلِكَ عَلَى النَّاسِ حَتَّى تَغَيَّرَتْ وُجُوهُهُمْ، قَالَ النَّبِيُّ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "من يأجوج ومأجوج تسعمائة وتسعة وتسعين ، وَمِنْكُمْ وَاحِدٌ، ثُمَّ أَنْتُمْ فِي النَّاسِ كَالشَّعْرَةِ السَّوْدَاءِ فِي جَنْبِ الثَّوْرِ الْأَبْيَضِ، أَوْ كَالشَّعْرَةِ الْبَيْضَاءِ فِي جَنْبِ الثَّوْرِ الْأَسْوَدِ، وَإِنِّي لَأَرْجُو أَنْ تَكُونُوا رُبُعَ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ". فَكَبَّرْنَا، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "ثُلُثُ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ". فَكَبَّرْنَا، ثُمَّ قَالَ: "شَطْرُ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ" فَكَبَّرْنَا .

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ أَيْضًا فِي غَيْرِ هَذَا الْمَوْضِعِ، وَمُسْلِمٌ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ .

الْحَدِيثُ الْخَامِسُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَمَّارُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ -ابْنُ أُخْتِ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ-وَعُبَيْدَةَ الْمَعْنَى، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الْأَحْوَصِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إن اللَّهَ يَبْعَثُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ مُنَادِيًا [يُنَادِي] : يَا آدَمُ، إِنْ اللَّهَ يَأْمُرُكَ أَنْ تَبْعَثَ بَعْثًا مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِكَ إِلَى النَّارِ، فَيَقُولُ آدَمُ: يَا رَبِّ، مَنْ هُمْ؟ فَيُقَالُ لَهُ: مِنْ كُلِّ مِائَةٍ تِسْعَةً وَتِسْعِينَ". فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْقَوْمِ: مَنْ هَذَا النَّاجِي مِنَّا بَعْدَ هَذَا يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ : "هَلْ تَدْرُونَ مَا أَنْتُمْ فِي النَّاسِ إِلَّا كَالشَّامَةِ فِي صَدْرِ الْبَعِيرِ" .

انْفَرَدَ بِهَذَا السَّنَدِ وَهَذَا السِّيَاقِ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ.

الْحَدِيثُ السَّادِسُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى، عَنْ حَاتِمِ بْنِ أَبِي صَغِيرَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي مُلَيْكَةَ؛ أَنَّ الْقَاسِمَ بْنَ مُحَمَّدٍ أَخْبَرَهُ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّكُمْ تُحْشَرُونَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ حُفاة عُرَاةً غُرْلًا". قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، الرِّجَالُ وَالنِّسَاءُ يَنْظُرُ بَعْضُهُمْ إِلَى بَعْضٍ؟ قَالَ: "يَا عَائِشَةُ، إِنَّ الْأَمْرَ أَشَدُّ مِنْ أَنْ يُهِمَّهُمْ ذَاكَ". أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ .

الْحَدِيثُ السَّابِعُ: قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ خَالِدِ بْنِ أَبِي عِمْران، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، هَلْ يَذْكُرُ الْحَبِيبُ حَبِيبَهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ؟ قَالَ: "يَا عَائِشَةُ، أَمَّا عِنْدَ ثَلَاثٍ فَلَا أَمَّا عِنْدَ الْمِيزَانِ حَتَّى يِثْقُلَ أَوْ يَخِفَّ، فَلَا. وَأَمَّا عِنْدَ تَطَايُرِ الْكُتُبِ فَإِمَّا يُعْطَى بِيَمِينِهِ أَوْ يُعْطَى بِشَمَالِهِ، فَلَا. وَحِينَ يَخْرُجُ عُنُق مِنَ النَّارِ فَيَنْطَوِي عَلَيْهِمْ، وَيَتَغَيَّظُ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَيَقُولُ ذَلِكَ الْعُنُقُ: وُكِّلْتُ بِثَلَاثَةٍ، وُكِّلْتُ بِثَلَاثَةٍ، وُكِّلْتُ بِثَلَاثَةٍ: وُكِّلْتُ بِمَنِ ادَّعَى مَعَ اللَّهِ إِلَهًا آخَرَ، وَوُكِّلْتُ بِمَنْ لَا يُؤْمِنُ بِيَوْمِ الْحِسَابِ، وَوُكِّلْتُ بِكُلِّ جَبَّارٍ عَنِيدٍ" قَالَ: "فَيَنْطَوِي عَلَيْهِمْ، وَيَرْمِيهِمْ فِي غَمَرَاتٍ، وَلِجَهَنَّمَ جِسْرٌ أَدَقُّ مِنَ الشِّعْرِ وَأَحَدُّ مِنَ السَّيْفِ، عَلَيْهِ كَلَالِيبُ وَحَسَكٌ يأخُذْنَ مَنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ، وَالنَّاسُ عَلَيْهِ كَالطَّرْفِ وَكَالْبَرْقِ وَكَالرِّيحِ، وَكَأَجَاوِيدِ الْخَيْلِ وَالرِّكَابِ، وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ يَقُولُونَ: رَبِّ، سَلِّم، سَلِّم. فَنَاجٍ مُسَلَّمٌ، وَمَخْدُوشٌ مُسَلَّمٌ، ومكَوّر فِي النَّارِ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ " .

وَالْأَحَادِيثُ فِي أَهْوَالِ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ وَالْآثَارُ كَثِيرَةٌ جِدًّا، لَهَا مَوْضِعٌ آخَرُ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنَّ زَلْزَلَةَ السَّاعَةِ شَيْءٌ عَظِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: أَمْرٌ كَبِيرٌ، وَخَطْبٌ جَلِيلٌ، وَطَارِقٌ مُفْظِعٌ، وَحَادِثٌ هَائِلٌ، وَكَائِنٌ عَجِيبٌ.

وَالزِّلْزَالُ : هُوَ مَا يَحْصُلُ لِلنُّفُوسِ مِنَ الْفَزَعِ، وَالرُّعْبِ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هُنَالِكَ ابْتُلِيَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ وَزُلْزِلُوا زِلْزَالا شَدِيدًا﴾ [الأحزاب: ١١] .

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تَرَوْنَهَا﴾ : هَذَا مِنْ بَابِ ضَمِيرِ الشَّأْنِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ مُفَسِّرًا لَهُ: ﴿تَذْهَلُ كُلُّ مُرْضِعَةٍ عَمَّا أَرْضَعَتْ﴾ أَيْ: تَشْتَغِلُ لِهَوْلِ مَا تَرَى عَنْ أَحَبِّ النَّاسِ إِلَيْهَا، وَالَّتِي هِيَ أَشْفَقُ النَّاسِ عَلَيْهِ، تَدْهَشُ عَنْهُ فِي حَالِ إِرْضَاعِهَا لَهُ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿كُلُّ مُرْضِعَةٍ﴾ ، وَلَمْ يَقِلْ: "مُرْضِعٍ" وَقَالَ: ﴿عَمَّا أَرْضَعَتْ﴾ أَيْ: عَنْ رَضِيعِهَا قَبْلَ فِطَامِهِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَضَعُ كُلُّ ذَاتِ حَمْلٍ حَمْلَهَا﴾ أَيْ: قَبْلَ تَمَامِهِ لِشِدَّةِ الْهَوْلِ، ﴿وَتَرَى النَّاسَ سُكَارَى﴾ وَقُرِئَ: "سَكْرَى" أَيْ: مِنْ شِدَّةِ الْأَمْرِ الَّذِي [قَدْ] صَارُوا فِيهِ قَدْ دَهِشَتْ عُقُولُهُمْ، وَغَابَتْ أَذْهَانُهُمْ، فَمَنْ رَآهُمْ حَسَبَ أَنَّهُمْ سُكارى، ﴿وَمَا هُمْ بِسُكَارَى وَلَكِنَّ عَذَابَ اللَّهِ شَدِيدٌ﴾ .

---

## 22:3-4 — verses 3-4 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says this in condemnation of one who denies the resurrection and rejects God's power to bring the dead to life, turning away from what God has revealed to His prophets, and following in his speech, his denial, and his disbelief every rebellious devil, whether of mankind or of the jinn. This is the state of the people of misguidance and innovation, those who turn away from the truth and follow falsehood: they abandon what God revealed to His Messenger of clear truth, and instead follow the sayings of the leaders of misguidance, those who call to innovation through desires and personal opinions. It is for this reason that He said concerning them and those like them: {And among mankind is he who disputes about God without knowledge}, that is, without sound knowledge, {and follows every rebellious devil, against whom it has been decreed}. Mujahid said: it means the devil, that is, it has been decreed against him by a decree of divine ordainment, {that whoever takes him as an ally}, that is, follows him and submits to his guidance, {then indeed he will lead him astray and guide him to the punishment of the Blaze}, that is, he leads him astray in this world and drives him in the Hereafter to the punishment of the Blaze, which is hot, painful, tormenting, and unsettling.

Al-Suddi said, on the authority of Abu Malik: this verse was revealed concerning al-Nadr ibn al-Harith. Ibn Jurayj said likewise.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Ka'b al-Makki said: a wicked man among the wicked of Quraysh said, "Tell us about your Lord: is He made of gold, or of silver, or of copper?" Then the sky made a crashing sound, a qa'qa'ah, and qa'qa'ah in the speech of the Arabs means thunder, and suddenly the crown of his skull was found fallen before him.

Layth ibn Abi Sulaym said, on the authority of Mujahid: a Jew came and said, "O Muhammad, tell us about your Lord: of what substance is He? Of pearl or of ruby?" He said: then a thunderbolt came and seized him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى ذَامًّا لِمَنْ كَذَّبَ بِالْبَعْثِ، وَأَنْكَرَ قُدْرَةَ اللَّهِ عَلَى إِحْيَاءِ الْمَوْتَى، مُعْرِضًا عَمَّا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى أَنْبِيَائِهِ، مُتَّبِعًا فِي قَوْلِهِ وَإِنْكَارِهِ وَكُفْرِهِ كُلَّ شَيْطَانٍ مَرِيدٍ، مِنَ الْإِنْسِ وَالْجِنِّ، وَهَذَا حَالُ أَهْلِ الضَّلَالِ وَالْبِدَعِ، الْمُعْرِضِينَ عَنِ الْحَقِّ، الْمُتَّبِعِينَ لِلْبَاطِلِ، يَتْرُكُونَ مَا أَنْزَلَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ الْمُبِينِ، وَيَتَّبِعُونَ أَقْوَالَ رُءُوسِ الضَّلَالَةِ، الدُّعَاةِ إِلَى الْبِدَعِ بِالْأَهْوَاءِ وَالْآرَاءِ، وَلِهَذَا قَالَ فِي شَأْنِهِمْ وَأَشْبَاهِهِمْ: ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يُجَادِلُ فِي اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ﴾ ، أَيْ: عِلْمٍ صَحِيحٍ، ﴿وَيَتَّبِعُ كُلَّ شَيْطَانٍ. مَرِيدٍ كُتِبَ عَلَيْهِ﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي الشَّيْطَانَ، يَعْنِي: كُتِبَ عَلَيْهِ كِتَابَةً قَدَرِيَّةً ﴿أَنَّهُ مَنْ تَوَلاهُ﴾ أَيِ: اتَّبَعَهُ وَقَلَّدَهُ، ﴿فَأَنَّهُ يُضِلُّهُ وَيَهْدِيهِ إِلَى عَذَابِ السَّعِيرِ﴾ أَيْ: يُضِلُّهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَيَقُودُهُ فِي الْآخِرَةِ إِلَى عَذَابِ السَّعِيرِ، وَهُوَ الْحَارُّ الْمُؤْلِمُ الْمُزْعِجُ الْمُقْلِقُ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ، عَنِ أَبِي مَالِكٍ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي النَّضْرِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ. وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ سَلْمٍ الْبَصْرِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ الْمَحْرَمِ أَبُو قَتَادَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمَعْمَرُ ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو كَعْبٍ الْمَكِّيُّ قَالَ: قَالَ خَبِيثٌ مِنْ خُبثاء قُرَيْشٍ: أَخْبِرْنَا عَنْ رَبِّكُمْ، مِنْ ذَهَبٍ هُوَ، أَوْ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ هُوَ، أَوْ مِنْ نُحَاسٍ هُوَ؟ فَقَعْقَعَتِ السَّمَاءُ قَعْقَعَةً -وَالْقَعْقَعَةُ فِي كَلَامِ الْعَرَبِ: الرَّعْدُ-فَإِذَا قِحْف رَأَسِهِ سَاقِطٌ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ.

وَقَالَ لَيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: جَاءَ يَهُودِيٌّ فَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، أَخْبِرْنَا عَنْ رَبِّكَ: مَنْ أَيِّ شَيْءٍ هُوَ؟ مِنْ دُرٍّ أَمْ مِنْ يَاقُوتٍ؟ قال: فجاءت صاعقة فأخذته.

---

## 22:5-7 — verses 5-7 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the one who opposes resurrection and denies the return, He mentioned the proof of His power over the return, through what is observed of His originating of creation. He said: {O mankind, if you are in doubt}, meaning in uncertainty, {concerning the resurrection}, which is the return and the rising of souls and bodies on the Day of Resurrection, {then indeed We created you from dust}, meaning the origin of His creating you was from dust, which is what He created Adam (peace be upon him) from, {then from a sperm-drop}, meaning then He made his offspring from an extract of despised fluid, {then from a clot, then from a lump of flesh}. That is because when the sperm-drop settles in the womb of the woman, it remains as such for forty days, with what gathers to it being added to it. Then it turns into a red clot by God's permission, and remains thus for forty days. Then it changes and becomes a lump of flesh, a piece of flesh having no shape or features. Then the shaping and delineation begins, and from it a head, two hands, a chest and belly, two thighs and two legs, and the rest of the organs are formed. Sometimes the woman miscarries it before the shaping and delineation, and sometimes she expels it after it has already taken on shape and features. This is why the Exalted said: {then from a clot, then from a lump of flesh, shaped and unshaped}, meaning as you observe it, {that We may make clear to you. And We cause to remain in the wombs whom We will for a specified term}, meaning sometimes it settles in the womb and the woman neither expels it nor miscarries it. As Mujahid said concerning His statement {shaped and unshaped}: it means the miscarriage, whether formed or not formed.

When forty days have passed over it while it is a lump of flesh, God Almighty sends an angel to it, who breathes the spirit into it, and shapes it as God, Mighty and Majestic, wills, whether beautiful or ugly, male or female, and He writes its provision and its term, and whether it is wretched or blessed. This is established in the two Sahihs, from the hadith of al-A'mash, from Zayd ibn Wahb, from Ibn Mas'ud, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ, who is the truthful one, the one who is believed, told us: "Verily the creation of each of you is gathered in his mother's belly for forty nights, then he is a clot for a like period, then he is a lump of flesh for a like period, then God sends the angel to him and he is commanded with four matters: to write his deeds, his term, his provision, and whether he is wretched or blessed. Then the spirit is breathed into him."

Ibn Jarir and Ibn Abi Hatim narrated, from the hadith of Dawud ibn Abi Hind, from al-Sha'bi, from Alqamah, from Abdullah [Ibn Mas'ud], who said: When the sperm-drop settles in the womb, an angel takes it in his palm and says: "O Lord, shaped or unshaped?" If it is said "unshaped," it does not become a living soul, and the wombs cast it out as blood. But if it is said "shaped," he says: "O Lord, male or female? Wretched or blessed? What is the term? What is the outcome? And in what land will it die?" Then it is said to the sperm-drop: "Who is your Lord?" It says: "God." It is said: "Who provides for you?" It says: "God." Then it is said to him: "Go to the Book, for you will find in it the account of this sperm-drop." He said: Then it is shaped, and it lives out its term, and eats its provision, and treads its path, until when its term comes it dies, and is buried in that place. Then Amir al-Sha'bi recited: {O mankind, if you are in doubt concerning the resurrection, then indeed We created you from dust, then from a sperm-drop, then from a clot, then from a lump of flesh, shaped and unshaped}. When it reaches the stage of a lump of flesh, it is turned over in the fourth creation and becomes a living soul. If it is unshaped, the wombs cast it out as blood, and if it is shaped, it is turned over in creation.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Muhammad ibn Abdullah ibn Yazid al-Muqri told us, Sufyan told us, from Amr ibn Dinar, from Abu al-Tufayl, from Hudhayfah ibn Usayd, tracing it back to the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "The angel enters upon the sperm-drop after it has settled in the womb, after forty or forty-five days, and says: 'O Lord, wretched or blessed?' God then says, and the two angels write. He says: 'Male or female?' God then says, and the two angels write. And his deeds, his outcome, his provision, and his term are written. Then the scrolls are folded up, and nothing is added to what is in them nor is anything diminished."

Muslim narrated it from the hadith of Sufyan ibn Uyaynah, and from other routes, from Abu al-Tufayl, with a similar meaning.

His statement: {then We bring you forth as a child}, meaning weak in body, hearing, sight, senses, physical strength, and reason. Then God gives him strength little by little, and is gentle with him, and his two parents show him compassion throughout the hours of night and the ends of the day. This is why He said: {then that you may reach your full strength}, meaning that the powers become complete and increase, and one reaches the prime of youth and the fairness of appearance.

{And among you is he who is taken in death}, meaning during his youth and the fullness of his strength, {and among you is he who is brought back to the most decrepit age}, which is old age, senility, and the weakening of strength, reason, and understanding, and the decline of one's condition through senility and feebleness of thought. This is why He said: {so that he knows nothing after having had knowledge}, just as the Exalted said: {God is He who created you from weakness, then made after weakness strength, then made after strength weakness and gray hair. He creates what He wills, and He is the Knowing, the Capable} [al-Rum: 54].

The Hafiz Abu Ya'la Ahmad ibn Ali ibn al-Muthanna al-Mawsili said in his Musnad: [chain] Mansur ibn Abi Muzahim told us, Khalid al-Zayyat told us, Dawud Abu Sulayman told me, from Abdullah ibn Abd al-Rahman ibn Ma'mar ibn Hazm al-Ansari, from Anas ibn Malik, raising the hadith, who said: "The newborn, until he reaches puberty, whatever good he does is written for his father or his mother, and whatever evil he does is not written against him nor against his parents. When he reaches puberty, God sets the pen running upon him, and the two angels who are with him are commanded to record and to be strict. When he reaches forty years of age in Islam, God secures him from the three afflictions: madness, leprosy, and vitiligo. When he reaches fifty, God lightens his reckoning. When he reaches sixty, God grants him a turning to Him in what He loves. When he reaches seventy, the people of heaven love him. When he reaches eighty, God records his good deeds and overlooks his bad deeds. When he reaches ninety, God forgives him what has gone before of his sin and what is to come, and grants him intercession for his household, and he becomes God's captive on His earth. When he reaches the most decrepit age, {so that he knows nothing after having had knowledge}, God records for him the like of what he used to do of good in his health, and if he does an evil deed it is not recorded against him."

This is a hadith that is extremely gharib (singular), and there is severe irregularity in it. Nevertheless, Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal narrated it in his Musnad both raised and halted (mawquf), saying:

[chain] Abu al-Nadr told us, al-Faraj told us, Muhammad ibn Amir told us, from Muhammad ibn Abdullah al-Amiri, from Amr ibn Ja'far, from Anas, who said: When a Muslim man reaches forty years of age, God secures him from the various afflictions, from madness, leprosy, and vitiligo. When he reaches fifty, God eases his reckoning. When he reaches sixty, God grants him a turning to Him for which He loves him. When he reaches seventy, God loves him and the people of heaven love him. When he reaches eighty, God accepts his good deeds and erases his bad deeds from him. When he reaches ninety, God forgives him what has gone before of his sin and what is to come, and he is named God's captive on the earth, and intercession is granted for his household.

Then he said: [chain] Hashim told us, al-Faraj told us, Muhammad ibn Abdullah al-Amiri told me, from Muhammad ibn Abdullah ibn Amr ibn Uthman, from Abdullah ibn Umar ibn al-Khattab, from the Prophet ﷺ, the like of it.

Imam Ahmad also narrated it: [chain] Anas ibn Iyad told us, Yusuf ibn Abi Dharrah al-Ansari told me, from Ja'far ibn Amr ibn Umayyah al-Damri, from Anas ibn Malik, that the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "There is no one who is granted long life in Islam for forty years but that God turns away from him three kinds of affliction: madness, leprosy, and vitiligo," and he mentioned the rest of the hadith, exactly as preceded.

Al-Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bazzar related it, from Abdullah ibn Shabib, from Abu Shaybah, from Abdullah ibn Abd al-Malik, from Abu Qatadah al-Udhri, from the nephew of al-Zuhri, from his uncle, from Anas ibn Malik, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There is no servant who reaches the age of forty years in Islam except that Allah turns away from him various kinds of affliction: madness, leprosy, and vitiligo. When he reaches fifty years, Allah eases the reckoning for him. When he reaches sixty years, Allah grants him the ability to turn to Him in repentance in a way He loves. When he reaches seventy, Allah forgives him what has passed of his sins and what is to come, and he is named the captive of Allah, and the people of heaven love him. When he reaches eighty, Allah accepts his good deeds and overlooks his evil deeds. When he reaches ninety, He forgives him what has passed of his sins and what is to come, and he is named the captive of Allah on His earth, and intercession is granted for him regarding the people of his household."

* *

His saying, {And you see the earth barren}: this is another proof of His, the Exalted's, power to bring the dead to life, just as He brings to life the dead, barren earth. It is the dry land in which there is no plant and nothing at all.

Qatadah said: dust-colored, crumbled. Al-Suddi said: dead.

{Then when We send down water upon it, it stirs and swells and grows every delightful kind}, meaning: when Allah sends down rain upon it, {it stirs}, that is, it moves and comes to life after its death, {and swells}, that is, it rises up when the moisture settles within it, then it grows what is in it of varieties and kinds, of fruits and crops, and different plants in the diversity of their colors, tastes, scents, forms, and benefits. For this reason the Exalted said: {and grows every delightful kind}, meaning: beautiful in appearance, pleasant in scent.

* *

His saying, {That is because Allah, He is the Truth}, meaning: the Creator, the Disposer, the One who does what He wills, {and that He gives life to the dead} [meaning: just as He brought the dead earth to life and caused these kinds to grow from it; {indeed, the One who gave it life is surely the One who gives life to the dead}], {indeed He is over all things capable} [Fussilat: 39]. So {His command, when He wills a thing, is only that He says to it "Be," and it is} [Ya-Sin: 82].

{And that the Hour is coming, there is no doubt in it}, meaning: it is certain to occur, there is no doubt or uncertainty in it, {and that Allah will resurrect those who are in the graves}, meaning: He will bring them back after they have become, in their graves, decayed bones, and bring them into existence after nonexistence, as the Exalted said: {And he presents for Us an example and forgets his own creation. He says, "Who will give life to bones when they are decayed?" Say, "He who created them the first time will give them life, and He is Knowing of every creation. He who made for you from the green tree fire, and behold, you kindle from it"} [Ya-Sin: 78-80]. And the verses on this subject are numerous.

Imam Ahmad said: Bahz related to us, Hammad ibn Salamah related to us, saying: Ya'la informed us, from Ata', from Waki' ibn Hudus, from his uncle Abu Razin al-Uqayli, whose name was Laqit ibn Amir, that he said: O Messenger of Allah, will all of us see our Lord, Mighty and Majestic, on the Day of Resurrection? And what is the sign of that in His creation? The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Does not each of you look at the moon when alone with it?" We said: Yes indeed. He said: "Then Allah is greater." He said: I said: O Messenger of Allah, how does Allah give life to the dead, and what is the sign of that in His creation? He said: "Have you not passed by the valley of your people when it was barren?" He said: Yes indeed. He said: "Then did you pass by it again when it was stirring with green growth?" He said: Yes indeed. He said: "Thus does Allah give life to the dead, and that is His sign in His creation."

Abu Dawud and Ibn Majah related it, from the hadith of Hammad ibn Salamah, with the same wording.

Then Imam Ahmad also related it: Ali ibn Ishaq related to us, Ibn al-Mubarak informed us, Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid ibn Jabir informed us, from Sulayman ibn Musa, from Abu Razin al-Uqayli, who said: I came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said: O Messenger of Allah, how does Allah give life to the dead? He said: "Have you passed by some land of yours when it was barren, then passed by it again when it was fertile?" He said: Yes. He said: "Such is the resurrection."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: my father related to us, Ubays ibn Marhum related to us, Bukayr ibn Abi al-Sumayt related to us, from Qatadah, from Abu al-Hajjaj, from Mu'adh ibn Jabal, who said: Whoever knows that Allah is the Manifest Truth, and that the Hour is coming with no doubt in it, and that Allah will resurrect those who are in the graves, will enter Paradise. [And Allah knows best.]

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى الْمُخَالِفَ لِلْبَعْثِ، الْمُنْكِرَ لِلْمَعَادِ، ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى الدَّلِيلَ عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ تَعَالَى عَلَى الْمَعَادِ، بِمَا يُشَاهَدُ مِنْ بَدْئِهِ لِلْخَلْقِ ، فَقَالَ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ فِي رَيْبٍ﴾ أَيْ: فِي شَكٍّ ﴿مِنَ الْبَعْثِ﴾ وَهُوَ الْمَعَادُ وَقِيَامُ الْأَرْوَاحِ وَالْأَجْسَادِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ﴿فَإِنَّا خَلَقْنَاكُمْ مِنْ تُرَابٍ﴾ أَيْ: أَصْلُ بَرْئه لَكُمْ مِنْ تُرَابٍ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي خَلَقَ مِنْهُ آدَمَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ ﴿ثُمَّ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: ثُمَّ جَعَلَ نَسْلَهُ مِنْ سُلَالَةٍ مِنْ مَاءٍ مَهِينٍ، ﴿ثُمَّ مِنْ عَلَقَةٍ ثُمَّ مِنْ مُضْغَةٍ﴾ ذَلِكَ أَنَّهُ إِذَا اسْتَقَرَّتِ النُّطْفَةُ فِي رَحِمِ الْمَرْأَةِ، مَكَثَتْ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا كَذَلِكَ، يُضَافُ إِلَيْهِ مَا يَجْتَمِعُ إِلَيْهَا، ثُمَّ تَنْقَلِبُ عَلَقَةً حَمْرَاءَ بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ، فَتَمْكُثُ كَذَلِكَ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، ثُمَّ تَسْتَحِيلُ فَتَصِيرُ مُضْغَةً -قِطْعَةً مِنْ لَحْمٍ لَا شَكْلَ فِيهَا وَلَا تَخْطِيطَ-ثُمَّ يُشْرَعُ فِي التَّشْكِيلِ وَالتَّخْطِيطِ، فَيُصَوَّرُ مِنْهَا رَأْسٌ وَيَدَانِ، وَصَدْرٌ وَبَطْنٌ، وَفَخْذَانِ وَرِجْلَانِ، وَسَائِرُ الْأَعْضَاءِ. فَتَارَةً تُسقطها الْمَرْأَةُ قَبْلَ التَّشْكِيلِ وَالتَّخْطِيطِ، وَتَارَةً تُلْقِيهَا وَقَدْ صَارَتْ ذَاتَ شَكْلٍ وَتَخْطِيطٍ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿ثُمَّ مِنْ عَلَقَةٍ ثُمَّ مِنْ مُضْغَةٍ مُخَلَّقَةٍ وَغَيْرِ مُخَلَّقَةٍ﴾ أَيْ: كَمَا تُشَاهِدُونَهَا، ﴿لِنُبَيِّنَ لَكُمْ وَنُقِرُّ فِي الأرْحَامِ مَا نَشَاءُ إِلَى أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى﴾ أَيْ: وَتَارَةً تَسْتَقِرُّ فِي الرَّحِمِ لَا تُلْقِيهَا الْمَرْأَةُ وَلَا تُسْقِطُهَا، كَمَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿مُخَلَّقَةٍ وَغَيْرِ مُخَلَّقَةٍ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ السَّقْطُ مَخْلُوقٌ وَغَيْرُ مَخْلُوقٍ. فَإِذَا مَضَى عَلَيْهَا أَرْبَعُونَ يَوْمًا، وَهِيَ مُضْغَةٌ، أَرْسَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى إِلَيْهَا مَلَكًا فَنَفَخَ فِيهَا الرَّوْحَ، وَسَوَّاهَا كَمَا يَشَاءُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ ، مِنْ حَسَنٍ وَقَبِيحٍ، وَذَكَرٍ وَأَنْثَى، وَكَتَبَ رِزْقَهَا وَأَجَلَهَا، وَشِقِّيٌ أَوْ سَعِيدٌ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ وَهْبٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ -وَهُوَ الصَّادِقُ الْمَصْدُوقُ-:"إِنَّ خَلْقَ أَحَدِكُمْ يُجمع فِي بَطْنِ أُمِّهِ أَرْبَعِينَ لَيْلَةً، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ عَلَقَةً مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ يَكُونُ مُضغة مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، ثُمَّ يَبْعَثُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ الْمَلَكَ فَيُؤْمَرُ بِأَرْبَعِ كَلَمَّاتٍ: بِكَتْبِ عَمَلِهِ وَأَجَلِهِ وَرِزْقِهِ، وَشَقِّيٌ أَوْ سَعِيدٌ، ثُمَّ يُنْفَخُ فِيهِ الرُّوحُ" .

وَرَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ حَدِيثِ دَاوُدَ بْنِ أَبِي هِنْدٍ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ علقمة، عن عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: النُّطْفَةُ إِذَا اسْتَقَرَّتْ فِي الرَّحِمِ، أَخَذَهَا مَلَكٌ بِكَفِّهِ قَالَ : يَا رَبِّ، مخلقة أو غير مُخَلَّقَةٍ؟ فَإِنْ قِيلَ: "غَيْرُ مُخَلَّقَةٍ" لَمْ تَكُنْ نَسَمَةٌ، وَقَذَفَتْهَا الْأَرْحَامُ دَمًا. وَإنْ قِيلَ: "مُخَلَّقَةٌ"، قَالَ: أَيْ رَبِّ، ذَكَرٌ أَوْ أَنْثَى؟ شَقِيٌّ أَوْ سَعِيدٌ؟ مَا الْأَجَلُ؟ وَمَا الْأَثَرُ؟ وَبِأَيِّ أَرْضٍ يَمُوتُ ؟ قَالَ: فَيُقَالُ لِلنُّطْفَةِ: مَنْ رَبُّكِ؟ فَتَقُولُ: اللَّهُ. فَيُقَالُ: مَنْ رَازِقُكِ؟ فَتَقُولُ: اللَّهُ. فيقال له: اذهب إلى الْكِتَابِ، فَإِنَّكَ سَتَجِدُ فِيهِ قِصَّةَ هَذِهِ النُّطْفَةِ. قَالَ: فَتُخْلَقُ فَتَعِيشُ فِي أَجَلِهَا، وَتَأْكُلُ رِزْقَهَا، وَتَطَأُ أَثَرَهَا، حَتَّى إِذَا جَاءَ أَجَلُهَا مَاتَتْ، فَدُفِنَتْ فِي ذَلِكَ الْمَكَانِ، ثُمَّ تَلَا عَامِرٌ الشَّعْبِيُّ: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ فِي رَيْبٍ مِنَ الْبَعْثِ فَإِنَّا خَلَقْنَاكُمْ مِنْ تُرَابٍ ثُمَّ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ ثُمَّ مِنْ عَلَقَةٍ ثُمَّ مِنْ مُضْغَةٍ مُخَلَّقَةٍ وَغَيْرِ مُخَلَّقَةٍ﴾ فَإِذَا بَلَغَتْ مُضْغَةً نُكِّسَتْ فِي الْخَلْقِ الرَّابِعِ فَكَانَتْ نَسَمَةً، فَإِنْ كَانَتْ غَيْرَ مُخَلَّقَةٍ قَذَفَتْهَا الْأَرْحَامُ دَمًا، وَإِنْ كَانَتْ مُخَلَّقَةً نُكِّسَتْ فِي الْخَلْقِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ يَزِيدَ الْمُقْرِئُ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ أَبِي الطُّفَيْلِ، عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ بْنِ أُسَيْدٍ -يَبْلُغُ بِهِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ-قَالَ: "يَدْخُلُ الْمَلَكُ عَلَى النُّطْفَةِ بَعْدَ مَا تَسْتَقِرُّ فِي الرَّحِمِ بِأَرْبَعِينَ أَوْ خَمْسٍ وَأَرْبَعِينَ، فَيَقُولُ: أَيْ رَبِّ، أَشَقِيٌّ أَمْ سَعِيدٌ؟ فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ، وَيَكْتُبَانِ، فَيَقُولُ: أَذَكَرٌ أَمْ أَنْثَى؟ فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ وَيَكْتُبَانِ، وَيُكْتَبُ عَمَلُهُ وَأَثَرُهُ وَرِزْقُهُ وَأَجَلُهُ، ثُمَّ تُطْوَى الصُّحُفُ، فَلَا يُزَادُ عَلَى مَا فِيهَا وَلَا يُنْتَقَصُ .

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، وَمِنْ طُرُقٍ أُخَرَ، عَنِ أَبِي الطُّفَيل، بِنَحْوِ مَعْنَاهُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ نُخْرِجُكُمْ طِفْلا﴾ أَيْ: ضَعِيفًا فِي بَدَنِهِ، وَسَمْعِهِ وَبَصَرِهِ وَحَوَاسِّهِ، وَبَطْشِهِ وَعَقْلِهِ. ثُمَّ يُعْطِيهِ اللَّهُ الْقُوَّةَ شَيْئًا فَشَيْئًا، وَيَلْطُفُ بِهِ، وَيَحْنُنْ عَلَيْهِ وَالِدِّيَةُ فِي آنَاءِ اللَّيْلِ وَأَطْرَافِ النَّهَارِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ثُمَّ لِتَبْلُغُوا أَشُدَّكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: يَتَكَامَلُ الْقُوَى وَيَتَزَايَدُ، وَيَصِلُ إِلَى عُنْفُوَانِ الشَّبَابِ وَحُسْنِ الْمَنْظَرِ.

﴿وَمِنْكُمْ مَنْ يُتَوَفَّى﴾ ، أَيْ: فِي حَالِ شَبَابِهِ وَقَوَاهُ، ﴿وَمِنْكُمْ مَنْ يُرَدُّ إِلَى أَرْذَلِ الْعُمُرِ﴾ ، وَهُوَ الشَّيْخُوخَةُ والهَرَم وَضَعْفُ الْقُوَّةِ وَالْعَقْلِ وَالْفَهْمِ، وَتَنَاقُصُ الْأَحْوَالِ مِنَ الخَرَف وَضَعْفِ الْفِكْرِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿لِكَيْلا يَعْلَمَ مِنْ بَعْدِ عِلْمٍ شَيْئًا﴾ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿اللَّهُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ ضَعْفٍ ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ضَعْفٍ قُوَّةً ثُمَّ جَعَلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ قُوَّةٍ ضَعْفًا وَشَيْبَةً يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ وَهُوَ الْعَلِيمُ الْقَدِيرُ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٥٤] .

وَقَدْ قَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى [أَحْمَدُ] بْنُ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْمُثَنَّى الْمَوْصِلِيُّ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا مَنْصُورُ بْنُ أَبِي مُزَاحِمٍ ، حَدَّثَنَا خَالِدٌ الزَّيَّاتُ، حَدَّثَنِي دَاوُدُ أَبُو سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ مَعْمَرِ ابن حَزْمٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ، عَنِ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ -رَفَعَ الْحَدِيثَ-قَالَ: "الْمَوْلُودُ حَتَّى يَبْلُغَ الْحِنْثَ، مَا عَمِلَ مِنْ حَسَنَةٍ، كُتِبَتْ لِوَالِدِهِ أَوْ لِوَالِدَتِهِ وَمَا عَمِلَ مِنْ سَيِّئَةٍ لَمْ تُكْتَبْ عَلَيْهِ وَلَا عَلَى وَالِدَيْهِ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ الْحِنْثَ جَرَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ الْقَلَمُ أُمِرَ الْمَلِكَانِ اللَّذَانِ مَعَهُ أَنْ يَحْفَظَا وَأَنْ يُشَدِّدَا، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ أَرْبَعِينَ سنة في الْإِسْلَامِ أَمَّنَهُ اللَّهُ مِنَ الْبَلَايَا الثَّلَاثِ: الْجُنُونُ، وَالْجُذَامُ، وَالْبَرَصُ. فَإِذَا بَلَغَ الْخَمْسِينَ، خَفَّفَ اللَّهُ حِسَابَهُ. فَإِذَا بَلَغَ سِتِّينَ رَزَقَهُ اللَّهُ الْإِنَابَةَ إِلَيْهِ بِمَا يُحِبُّ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ السَّبْعِينَ أَحَبَّهُ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ، فَإِذَا بَلَّغَ الثَّمَانِينَ كَتَبَ اللَّهُ حسناته وتجاوز عن سيئاته، فإذا بلغ التسعين غَفَرَ اللَّهُ لَهُ مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ ذَنْبِهِ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ، وَشَفَّعَهُ فِي أَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ، وَكَانَ أَسِيرَ اللَّهِ فِي أَرْضِهِ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ أَرْذَلَ الْعُمُرِ ﴿لِكَيْلا يَعْلَمَ مِنْ بَعْدِ عِلْمٍ شَيْئًا﴾ كَتَبَ اللَّهُ لَهُ مِثْلَ مَا كَانَ يَعْمَلُ فِي صِحَّتِهِ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ، فَإِذَا عَمِلَ سَيِّئَةً لَمْ تُكْتَبْ عَلَيْهِ" .

هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا، وَفِيهِ نَكَارَةٌ شَدِيدَةٌ. وَمَعَ هَذَا قَدْ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ مَرْفُوعًا وَمَوْقُوفًا فَقَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو النَّضْرِ، حَدَّثَنَا الْفَرَجُ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَامِرٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْعَامِرِيِّ ، عَنْ عَمْرِو بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، عَنْ أَنْسٍ قَالَ: إِذَا بَلَغَ الرَّجُلُ الْمُسْلِمُ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً، أَمَّنَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْ أَنْوَاعِ الْبَلَايَا، مِنَ الْجُنُونِ وَالْجُذَامِ وَالْبَرَصِ ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ الْخَمْسِينَ لَيَّن اللَّهُ حِسَابَهُ، وَإِذَا بَلَغَ السِّتِّينَ رَزَقَهُ اللَّهُ إِنَابَةً يُحِبُّهُ عَلَيْهَا، وَإِذَا بَلَغَ السَّبْعِينَ أَحَبَّهُ اللَّهُ، وَأَحَبَّهُ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ، وَإِذَا بَلَغَ الثَّمَانِينَ تَقَبَّلَ اللَّهُ حَسَنَاتِهِ، وَمَحَا عَنْهُ سَيِّئَاتِهِ، وَإِذَا بَلَغَ التِّسْعِينَ غَفَرَ اللَّهُ لَهُ مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ ذَنْبِهِ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ، وسمي أسير اللَّهِ فِي الْأَرْضِ، وَشُفِّعَ فِي أَهْلِهِ .

ثُمَّ قَالَ: حَدَّثَنَا هَاشِمٌ، حَدَّثَنَا الْفَرَجُ، حَدَّثَنِي مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْعَامِرِيُّ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عُثْمَانَ، عَنْ عبد الله بن عمر بن الخطاب، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، مِثْلَهُ .

وَرَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا أَنَسُ بْنُ عِيَاضٍ، حَدَّثَنِي يُوسُفُ بْنُ أَبِي ذَرَّةَ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ الضَّمْري، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا مِنْ مُعَمَّرٍ يُعَمَّرُ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً، إِلَّا صَرَفَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ ثَلَاثَةَ أَنْوَاعٍ مِنَ الْبَلَاءِ: الْجُنُونُ وَالْجُذَامُ وَالْبَرَصُ ..... وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْحَدِيثِ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ سَوَاءً .

وَرَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْبَزَّارُ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ شَبِيبٍ، عَنِ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ ، عَنِ أَبِي قَتَادَةَ العُذْري، عَنِ ابْنِ أَخِي الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ عَمِّهِ، عَنْ أَنَسِ بْنِ مَالِكٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا مِنْ عَبْدٍ يُعَمَّرُ فِي الْإِسْلَامِ أَرْبَعِينَ سَنَةً، إِلَّا صَرَفَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ أَنْوَاعًا مِنَ الْبَلَاءِ: الْجُنُونُ وَالْجُذَامُ وَالْبَرَصُ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ خَمْسِينَ سَنَةً لَيَّنَ اللَّهُ لَهُ الْحِسَابَ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ سِتِّينَ سَنَةً رَزَقَهُ اللَّهُ الْإِنَابَةَ إِلَيْهِ بِمَا يُحِبُّ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ سَبْعِينَ غَفَرَ اللَّهُ لَهُ مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ ذَنْبِهِ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ، وسمي أَسِيرَ اللَّهِ، وَأَحَبَّهُ أَهْلُ السَّمَاءِ ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ الثَّمَانِينَ تَقَبَّلَ اللَّهُ مِنْهُ حَسَنَاتِهِ وَتَجَاوُزَ عَنْ سَيِّئَاتِهِ، فَإِذَا بَلَغَ التِّسْعِينَ غَفَر لَهُ مَا تَقَدَّمَ مِنْ ذَنْبِهِ وَمَا تَأَخَّرَ، وسُمي أسير اللَّهِ فِي أَرْضِهِ، وَشُفِّعَ فِي أَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَتَرَى الأرْضَ هَامِدَةً﴾ : هَذَا دَلِيلٌ آخَرُ عَلَى قُدْرَتِهِ تَعَالَى عَلَى إِحْيَاءِ الْمَوْتَى، كَمَا يُحْيِي الْأَرْضَ الْمَيْتَةَ الْهَامِدَةَ، وَهِيَ القحلَة الَّتِي لَا نَبْتَ فِيهَا وَلَا شَيْءَ .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: غَبْرَاءُ مُتَهَشِّمَةٌ. وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: مَيْتَةٌ.

﴿فَإِذَا أَنزلْنَا عَلَيْهَا الْمَاءَ اهْتَزَّتْ وَرَبَتْ وَأَنْبَتَتْ مِنْ كُلِّ زَوْجٍ بَهِيجٍ﴾ أَيْ: فَإِذَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهَا الْمَطَرَ ﴿اهْتَزَّتْ﴾ أَيْ: تَحَرَّكَتْ وَحَيِيَتْ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهَا، ﴿وَرَبَتْ﴾ أَيِ: ارْتَفَعَتْ لَمَّا سَكَنَ فِيهَا الثَّرَى، ثُمَّ أَنْبَتَتْ مَا فِيهَا مِنَ الْأَلْوَانِ وَالْفُنُونِ، مِنْ ثِمَارٍ وَزُرُوعٍ، وَأَشْتَاتِ النَّبَاتَاتِ فِي اخْتِلَافِ أَلْوَانِهَا وَطَعُومِهَا، وَرَوَائِحِهَا وَأَشْكَالِهَا وَمَنَافِعِهَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَأَنْبَتَتْ مِنْ كُلِّ زَوْجٍ بَهِيجٍ﴾ أَيْ: حَسَنِ الْمَنْظَرِ طَيِّبِ الرِّيحِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ذَلِكَ بِأَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْحَقُّ﴾ أَيِ: الْخَالِقُ الْمُدَبِّرُ الْفَعَّالُ لِمَا يَشَاءُ، ﴿وَأَنَّهُ يُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى﴾ [أَيْ: كَمَا أَحْيَا الْأَرْضَ الْمَيْتَةَ وَأَنْبَتَ مِنْهَا هَذِهِ الْأَنْوَاعَ؛ ﴿إِنَّ الَّذِي أَحْيَاهَا لَمُحْيِي الْمَوْتَى﴾ ] ، ﴿إِنَّهُ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ﴾ [فُصِّلَتْ: ٣٩] فَـ ﴿إِنَّمَا أَمْرُهُ إِذَا أَرَادَ شَيْئًا أَنْ يَقُولَ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ﴾ [يس: ٨٢] .

﴿وَأَنَّ السَّاعَةَ آتِيَةٌ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: كَائِنَةٌ لَا شَكَّ فِيهَا وَلَا مِرْيَةَ، ﴿وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ يَبْعَثُ مَنْ فِي الْقُبُورِ﴾ أَيْ: يُعِيدُهُمْ بَعْدَ مَا صَارُوا فِي قُبُورِهِمْ رِمَمًا، وَيُوجِدُهُمْ بَعْدَ الْعَدَمِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَضَرَبَ لَنَا مَثَلا وَنَسِيَ خَلْقَهُ قَالَ مَنْ يُحْيِي الْعِظَامَ وَهِيَ رَمِيمٌ. قُلْ يُحْيِيهَا الَّذِي أَنْشَأَهَا أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ خَلْقٍ عَلِيمٌ. الَّذِي جَعَلَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الشَّجَرِ الأخْضَرِ نَارًا فَإِذَا أَنْتُمْ مِنْهُ تُوقِدُونَ﴾ [يس: ٧٨ -٨٠] وَالْآيَاتُ فِي هَذَا كَثِيرَةٌ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا بَهز ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ قَالَ: أَنْبَأَنَا يَعْلَى عَنْ عَطَاءٍ، عَنْ وَكِيعِ بْنِ حُدُس ، عَنْ عَمِّهِ أَبِي رَزين الْعُقَيْلِيِّ -وَاسْمُهُ لَقِيط بْنُ عَامِرٍ -أَنَّهُ قَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَكُلُّنَا يَرَى رَبَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ؟ وَمَا آيَةُ ذَلِكَ فِي خَلْقِهِ؟ فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَلَيْسَ كُلُّكُمْ يَنْظُرُ إِلَى الْقَمَرِ مُخْليا بِهِ؟ " قُلْنَا: بَلَى. قَالَ: "فَاللَّهُ أَعْظَمُ". قَالَ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ يُحْيِي اللَّهُ الْمَوْتَى، وَمَا آيَةُ ذَلِكَ فِي خَلْقِهِ؟ قَالَ: "أَمَا مَرَرْتَ بِوَادِي أَهْلِكَ مَحْلًا " قَالَ: بَلَى. قَالَ: "ثُمَّ مَرَرْتَ بِهِ يَهْتَزُّ خَضِرًا؟ ". قَالَ: بَلَى. قَالَ: "فَكَذَلِكَ يُحْيِي اللَّهُ الْمَوْتَى، وَذَلِكَ آيَتُهُ فِي خَلْقِهِ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ حَمَّادِ بْنِ سَلَمَةَ، بِهِ .

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، أَنْبَأَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ يَزِيدَ بْنِ جَابِرٍ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنِ أَبِي رَزين العُقَيْلي قَالَ: أَتَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم فقلت: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَيْفَ يُحْيِي اللَّهُ الْمَوْتَى؟ قَالَ: "أَمَرَرْتَ بِأَرْضٍ من أرضك مُجْدبةً، ثم مررت بها مُخْصِبَةً؟ " قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: "كَذَلِكَ النُّشُورُ" .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيس بْنُ مَرْحُومٍ، حَدَّثَنَا بُكَيْر بْنُ أَبِي السُّمَيْط، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ، عَنِ أَبِي الْحَجَّاجِ، عَنْ مُعَاذِ بْنِ جَبَلٍ قَالَ: مَنْ عَلِمَ أَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ الْحَقُّ الْمُبِينُ، وَأَنَّ السَّاعَةَ آتِيَةٌ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهَا، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ يَبْعَثُ مَنْ فِي الْقُبُورِ -دَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ. [وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ] .

---

## 22:8-10 — verses 8-10 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When God, exalted is He, mentioned the state of the misguided, ignorant imitators in His saying: {And among mankind is he who disputes concerning God without knowledge and follows every rebellious devil}, He mentioned in this passage the state of the callers to misguidance among the leaders of disbelief and innovation, saying: {And among mankind is he who disputes concerning God without knowledge or guidance or an illuminating book}. That is, without sound reason and without sound, explicit transmitted proof, but rather by mere opinion and desire.

Regarding His saying {thani itfihi} (twisting his side), Ibn Abbas and others said: it means being arrogant toward the truth when called to it. Mujahid, Qatada, and Malik, from Zayd ibn Aslam, said: {thani itfihi} means twisting his neck, that is, his throat, meaning he turns his neck away in arrogance from the truth he is called to. This is like His saying, exalted is He: {And in Moses, when We sent him to Pharaoh with clear authority. But he turned away in his strength and said, a magician or a madman} [al-Dhariyat: 38-39]. And He, exalted is He, said: {And when it is said to them, come to what God has revealed and to the Messenger, you see the hypocrites turning away from you in aversion} [al-Nisa: 61]. And He said: {And when it is said to them, come, the Messenger of God will ask forgiveness for you, they turn their heads aside and you see them turning away while they are arrogant} [al-Munafiqun: 5]. And Luqman said to his son: {And do not turn your cheek away from people} [Luqman: 18], meaning, do not turn it away from them in arrogance toward them. And He, exalted is He, said: {And when Our verses are recited to him, he turns away in arrogance as if he had not heard them, as if there were a deafness in his ears; so give him tidings of a painful punishment} [Luqman: 7].

Regarding His saying {to lead astray from the path of God}: some said this is the lam of consequence (lam al-'aqibah), because that outcome may not have been intended by the one acting. It is also possible that it is the lam of causation (lam al-ta'lil). Then, either what is meant by it refers to those who are obstinately opposed to the truth, or what is meant is that this one who does this, We have simply formed him upon this character which makes him one of those who lead others astray from the path of God.

Then He, exalted is He, said: {For him in this world is disgrace}, that is, humiliation and abasement, just as when he was arrogant toward the signs of God, God made him meet with humiliation in this world, and punished him in it before the Hereafter, because this world was his greatest concern and the full extent of his knowledge. {And We will make him taste on the Day of Resurrection the punishment of the burning. That is for what your hands have sent forth}.

That is, this will be said to him in rebuke and reproach: {and that God is not unjust to His servants}, like His saying, exalted is He: {Seize him and drag him into the midst of the Blazing Fire. Then pour over his head the punishment of scalding water. Taste! Indeed you are the mighty, the noble! Indeed this is what you used to doubt} [al-Dukhan: 47-50].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] al-Hasan said: it has reached me that one of them will be burned seventy thousand times in a single day.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى حَالَ الضُّلَّالِ الْجُهَّالِ الْمُقَلِّدِينَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يُجَادِلُ فِي اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ وَيَتَّبِعُ كُلَّ شَيْطَانٍ مَرِيدٍ﴾ ، ذَكَرَ فِي هَذِهِ حَالَ الدُّعَاةِ إِلَى الضَّلَالِ مِنْ رُءُوسِ الْكُفْرِ وَالْبِدَعِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يُجَادِلُ فِي اللَّهِ بِغَيْرِ عِلْمٍ وَلا هُدًى وَلا كِتَابٍ مُنِيرٍ﴾ أَيْ: بِلَا عَقْلٍ صَحِيحٍ، وَلَا نَقْلٍ صَحِيحٍ صَرِيحٍ، بَلْ بِمُجَرَّدِ الرَّأْيِ وَالْهَوَى.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثَانِيَ عِطْفِهِ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ وَغَيْرُهُ: مُسْتَكْبِرًا عَنِ الْحَقِّ إِذَا دُعِيَ إِلَيْهِ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَمَالِكٌ عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿ثَانِيَ عِطْفِهِ﴾ أَيْ: لَاوِيَ عُنُقِهِ، وَهِيَ رَقَبَتُهُ، يَعْنِي: يُعْرِضُ عَمَّا يُدْعَى إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْحَقِّ رقَبَته اسْتِكْبَارًا، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَفِي مُوسَى إِذْ أَرْسَلْنَاهُ إِلَى فِرْعَوْنَ بِسُلْطَانٍ مُبِينٍ. فَتَوَلَّى بِرُكْنِهِ وَقَالَ سَاحِرٌ أَوْ مَجْنُونٌ﴾ [الذَّارِيَاتِ: ٣٨، ٣٩] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَوْا إِلَى مَا أَنزلَ اللَّهُ وَإِلَى الرَّسُولِ رَأَيْتَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ يَصُدُّونَ عَنْكَ صُدُودًا﴾ [النِّسَاءِ: ٦١] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَوْا يَسْتَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ لَوَّوْا رُءُوسَهُمْ وَرَأَيْتَهُمْ يَصُدُّونَ وَهُمْ مُسْتَكْبِرُونَ﴾ [الْمُنَافِقُونَ: ٥] : وَقَالَ لُقْمَانُ لِابْنِهِ: ﴿وَلا تُصَعِّرْ خَدَّكَ لِلنَّاسِ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ١٨] أَيْ: تُمِيلُهُ عَنْهُمُ اسْتِكْبَارًا عَلَيْهِمْ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا تُتْلَى عَلَيْهِ آيَاتُنَا وَلَّى مُسْتَكْبِرًا كَأَنْ لَمْ يَسْمَعْهَا كَأَنَّ فِي أُذُنَيْهِ وَقْرًا فَبَشِّرْهُ بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ﴾ [لُقْمَانَ: ٧] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لِيُضِلَّ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ﴾ : قَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: هَذِهِ لَامُ الْعَاقِبَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَدْ لَا يُقْصَدُ ذَلِكَ، وَيُحْتَمَلُ أَنْ تَكُونَ لَامَ التَّعْلِيلِ. ثُمَّ إِمَّا أَنْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ بِهَا الْمُعَانِدِينَ ، أَوْ يَكُونَ الْمُرَادُ بِهَا أَنَّ هَذَا الْفَاعِلَ لِهَذَا إِنَّمَا جَبَلْنَاهُ عَلَى هَذَا الْخُلُقِ الَّذِي يَجْعَلُهُ مِمَّنْ يُضِلُّ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ.

ثُمَّ قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا خِزْيٌ﴾ وَهُوَ الْإِهَانَةُ وَالذُّلُّ، كَمَا أَنَّهُ لَمَّا اسْتَكْبَرَ عَنِ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ لَقَّاه اللَّهُ الْمَذَلَّةَ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَعَاقَبَهُ فِيهَا قَبْلَ الْآخِرَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهَا أَكْبَرُ هَمّه وَمَبْلَغُ عِلْمِهِ، ﴿وَنُذِيقُهُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَذَابَ الْحَرِيقِ. ذَلِكَ بِمَا قَدَّمَتْ يَدَاكَ﴾

أَيْ: يُقَالُ لَهُ هَذَا تَقْرِيعًا وَتَوْبِيخًا، ﴿وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ لَيْسَ بِظَلامٍ لِلْعَبِيدِِ﴾ كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿خُذُوهُ فَاعْتِلُوهُ إِلَى سَوَاءِ الْجَحِيمِ. ثُمَّ صُبُّوا فَوْقَ رَأْسِهِ مِنْ عَذَابِ الْحَمِيمِ. ذُقْ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْعَزِيزُ الْكَرِيمُ. إِنَّ هَذَا مَا كُنْتُمْ بِهِ تَمْتَرُونَ﴾ [الدُّخَانِ: ٤٧ -٥٠] .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنِ الصَّبَّاحِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، أَنْبَأَنَا هِشَامٌ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّ أَحَدَهُمْ يُحرق فِي الْيَوْمِ سَبْعِينَ أَلْفَ مَرَّةٍ.

---

## 22:11-13 — verses 11-13 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Mujahid, Qatadah, and others said: {on a harf (edge/side)} means: in doubt.

Others said: on an edge, taken from "harf al-jabal" (the edge of the mountain), meaning its side, that is, he entered into the religion on the margin of it. If he found what he liked, he settled, and if not, he pulled away.

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] Ibrahim ibn al-Harith told us, Yahya ibn Abi Bukayr told us, Isra'il told us, from Abu Hasin, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {And among mankind is he who worships Allah upon a harf}: he said: a man would come to Madinah, and if his wife bore him a son and his horses foaled well, he would say, "This is a good religion." But if his wife did not bear a child and his horses did not foal, he would say, "This is a bad religion."

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ali ibn al-Husayn told us, Ahmad ibn Abd al-Rahman told us, my father told me, from his father, from Ash'ath ibn Ishaq al-Qummi, from Ja'far ibn Abi al-Mughirah, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: some of the Bedouin used to come to the Prophet ﷺ and embrace Islam. When they returned to their lands, if they found a year of rain, a year of abundance, and a year of good births, they would say, "Indeed this religion of ours is truly good, so hold fast to it." But if they found a year of drought, a year of bad births, and a year of famine, they would say, "There is no good in this religion of ours." So Allah revealed to His Prophet: {And among mankind is he who worships Allah upon a harf; if good befalls him he is content with it, but if a trial befalls him he turns away on his face}.

Al-'Awfi reported from Ibn Abbas: one of them, when he came to Madinah, which was a land of disease, if his body remained healthy there, and his mare foaled a fine colt, and his wife bore him a son, he would be pleased and settle into contentment with it, and say, "I have received nothing but good since I have been upon this religion of mine." But if a fitnah befell him, and fitnah here means affliction, that is, if the sickness of Madinah struck him, and his wife bore a daughter, and charity was delayed from reaching him, Satan would come to him and say: "By Allah, you have received nothing but harm since you have been upon this religion of yours." That is the fitnah.

Qatadah, al-Dahhak, Ibn Jurayj, and several others among the predecessors mentioned the like of this in explaining this verse.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: he is the hypocrite. If his worldly affairs go well, he continues in worship, but if his worldly affairs turn bad and change, he turns away, for he does not persist in worship except for the sake of what is good for him in this world. So if a trial, hardship, test, or constriction befalls him, he abandons his religion and returns to disbelief.

Mujahid said regarding His statement {he turns away on his face}: meaning, he apostatizes into disbelief.

Concerning His statement {he loses this world and the Hereafter}: meaning, he gains nothing at all from this world, and as for the Hereafter, he has disbelieved in Allah the Almighty, so he is there in the utmost of wretchedness and disgrace. That is why He said: {that is the manifest loss}, meaning, this is the tremendous loss, the losing transaction.

Concerning His statement {He calls upon, besides Allah, that which can neither harm him nor benefit him}: meaning, idols and rivals to Allah, which he cries out to for help, seeks victory from, and seeks provision from, yet they can neither benefit him nor harm him. {That is the far straying. He calls upon one whose harm is nearer than his benefit}, meaning, its harm to him in this world, before the Hereafter, is nearer than its benefit to him in it, while in the Hereafter its harm is certain and assured.

Concerning His statement {What an evil mawla (protector/patron), and what an evil ashir (companion)}: Mujahid said: it refers to the idol, meaning, evil indeed is this thing he called upon besides Allah as a mawla, that is, as a protector and helper, {and what an evil ashir}, meaning, the one he mixes and associates with.

Ibn Jarir preferred that what is meant is: evil indeed as a cousin and companion is the one who worships [Allah] upon a harf, {if good befalls him he is content with it, but if a trial befalls him he turns away on his face}.

But the statement of Mujahid, that what is meant is the idol, is more fitting and closer to the flow of the discourse. And Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا: ﴿عَلَى حَرْفٍ﴾ : عَلَى شَكٍّ .

وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُمْ: عَلَى طَرَفٍ. وَمِنْهُ حَرْفُ الْجَبَلِ، أَيْ: طَرَفَهُ، أَيْ: دَخَلَ فِي الدِّينِ عَلَى طَرَفٍ، فَإِنْ وَجَدَ مَا يُحِبُّهُ اسْتَقَرَّ، وَإِلَّا انْشَمَرَ.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ أَبِي بُكَيْر ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْرَائِيلُ، عَنْ أَبِي حَصِين، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَعْبُدُ اللَّهَ عَلَى حَرْفٍ﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ الرَّجُلُ يَقدم الْمَدِينَةَ، فَإِنْ وَلَدَتِ امْرَأَتُهُ غُلَامًا، ونُتِجَت خيلُه، قَالَ: هَذَا دِينٌ صَالِحٌ. وَإِنْ لَمْ تَلِدِ امْرَأَتُهُ، وَلَمْ تُنتَج خَيْلُهُ قَالَ: هَذَا دِينٌ سُوءٌ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَشْعَثَ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ القُمِّي، عَنْ جَعْفَرِ بْنِ أَبِي الْمُغِيرَةِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: كَانَ نَاسٌ مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ يَأْتُونَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فيُسْلِمون، فَإِذَا رَجَعُوا إِلَى بِلَادِهِمْ، فَإِنْ وَجَدُوا عَامَ غَيث وَعَامَ خِصْبٍ وَعَامَ وَلَادٍ حَسَنٍ، قَالُوا: "إِنَّ دِينَنَا هَذَا لَصَالِحٌ، فتمَسَّكُوا بِهِ". وَإِنْ وَجَدُوا عَامَ جُدوبة وَعَامَ وِلَادٍ سَوء وَعَامَ قَحْطٍ، قَالُوا: "مَا فِي دِينِنَا هَذَا خَيْرٌ". فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى نَبِيِّهِ: ﴿وَمِنَ النَّاسِ مَنْ يَعْبُدُ اللَّهَ عَلَى حَرْفٍ فَإِنْ أَصَابَهُ خَيْرٌ اطْمَأَنَّ بِهِ وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ فِتْنَةٌ انْقَلَبَ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: كَانَ أَحَدُهُمْ إِذَا قَدم الْمَدِينَةَ، وَهِيَ أَرْضٌ وَبِيئَةٌ ، فَإِنْ صَحَّ بِهَا جِسْمُهُ، ونُتِجت فَرَسُهُ مُهْرًا حَسَنًا، وَوَلَدَتِ امْرَأَتُهُ غُلَامًا، رَضِيَ بِهِ وَاطْمَأَنَّ إِلَيْهِ، وَقَالَ: "مَا أَصَبْتُ مُنْذُ كنتُ عَلَى دِينِي هَذَا إِلَّا خَيْرًا". وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ فِتْنَةٌ -وَالْفِتْنَةُ: الْبَلَاءُ-أَيْ: وَإِنْ أَصَابَهُ وَجَعُ المدينة، وَوَلَدَتِ امْرَأَتُهُ جَارِيَةً، وَتَأَخَّرَتْ عَنْهُ الصَّدَقَةُ، أَتَاهُ الشَّيْطَانُ فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ مَا أَصَبْتُ مُنْذُ كُنْتُ عَلَى دِينِكَ هَذَا إِلَّا شَرًّا. وَذَلِكَ الْفِتْنَةُ.

وَهَكَذَا ذَكَرَ قَتَادَةُ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَابْنُ جُريج، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ، فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: هُوَ الْمُنَافِقُ، إِنْ صَلُحَتْ لَهُ دُنْيَاهُ أَقَامَ عَلَى الْعِبَادَةِ، وَإِنْ فَسَدَتْ عَلَيْهِ دُنْيَاهُ وَتَغَيَّرَتْ، انْقَلَبَ فَلَا يُقِيمُ عَلَى الْعِبَادَةِ إِلَّا لِمَا صَلُحَ مِنْ دُنْيَاهُ، فَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ فِتْنَةٌ أَوْ شِدَّةٌ أَوِ اخْتِبَارٌ أَوْ ضِيقٌ، تَرَكَ دِينَهُ وَرَجَعَ إِلَى الْكُفْرِ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿انْقَلَبَ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ﴾ أَيِ: ارْتَدَّ كَافِرًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿خَسِرَ الدُّنْيَا وَالآخِرَةَ﴾ أَيْ: فَلَا هُوَ حَصَل مِنَ الدُّنْيَا عَلَى شَيْءٍ، وَأَمَّا الْآخِرَةُ فَقَدْ كَفَرَ بِاللَّهِ الْعَظِيمِ، فَهُوَ فِيهَا فِي غَايَةِ الشَّقَاءِ وَالْإِهَانَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿ذَلِكَ هُوَ الْخُسْرَانُ الْمُبِينُ﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ هِيَ الْخَسَارَةُ الْعَظِيمَةُ، وَالصَّفْقَةُ الْخَاسِرَةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَدْعُو مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يَضُرُّهُ وَمَا لَا يَنْفَعُهُ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْأَصْنَامِ وَالْأَنْدَادِ، يَسْتَغِيثُ بِهَا وَيَسْتَنْصِرُهَا وَيَسْتَرْزِقُهَا، وَهِيَ لَا تَنْفَعُهُ وَلَا تَضُرُّهُ، ﴿ذَلِكَ هُوَ الضَّلالُ الْبَعِيدُ. يَدْعُو لَمَنْ ضَرُّهُ أَقْرَبُ مِنْ نَفْعِهِ﴾ أَيْ: ضَرَرُهُ فِي الدُّنْيَا قَبْلَ الْآخِرَةِ أَقْرَبُ مِنْ نَفْعِهِ فِيهَا، وَأَمَّا فِي الْآخِرَةِ فَضَرَرُهُ مُحَقَّقٌ مُتَيَقَّنٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَبِئْسَ الْمَوْلَى وَلَبِئْسَ الْعَشِيرُ﴾ : قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي الْوَثَنَ، يَعْنِي: بِئْسَ هَذَا الَّذِي دَعَا بِهِ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَوْلًى، يَعْنِي: وَلِيًّا وَنَاصِرًا، ﴿وَلَبِئْسَ الْعَشِيرُ﴾ وَهُوَ الْمُخَالِطُ وَالْمُعَاشِرُ.

وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ: لَبِئْسَ ابْنُ الْعَمِّ وَالصَّاحِبُ مَنْ يَعْبُدُ [اللَّهَ] عَلَى حَرْفٍ، ﴿فَإِنْ أَصَابَهُ خَيْرٌ اطْمَأَنَّ بِهِ وَإِنْ أَصَابَتْهُ فِتْنَةٌ انْقَلَبَ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ﴾

وَقَوْلُ مُجَاهِدٍ: إِنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِهِ الْوَثَنُ، أَوْلَى وَأَقْرَبُ إِلَى سِيَاقِ الْكَلَامِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 22:14 — verse 14

### Translation

When He mentioned the people of misguidance, the wretched ones, He turned to mention the righteous ones, the fortunate ones, those who believed with their hearts and confirmed their faith with their deeds, so they performed righteous works of every kind of good deed [and abandoned wrongful acts]. This earned them the reward of dwelling in the elevated ranks, in the gardens of Paradise.

And when He mentioned that He led those astray and guided these, He said: {Indeed, Allah does what He wills}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ أَهْلَ الضَّلَالَةِ الْأَشْقِيَاءَ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ الْأَبْرَارِ السُّعَدَاءِ، مِنَ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِقُلُوبِهِمْ، وَصَدَّقُوا إِيمَانَهُمْ بِأَفْعَالِهِمْ، فَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ مِنْ جَمِيعِ أَنْوَاعِ الْقُرُبَاتِ، [وَتَرَكُوا الْمُنْكَرَاتِ] فَأَوْرَثَهُمْ ذَلِكَ سُكْنَى الدَّرَجَاتِ الْعَالِيَاتِ، فِي رَوْضَاتِ الْجَنَّاتِ.

وَلَمَّا ذَكَرَ أَنَّهُ أَضَلَّ أُولَئِكَ، وَهَدَى هَؤُلَاءِ، قَالَ: ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَفْعَلُ مَا يُرِيدُ﴾

---

## 22:15-16 — verses 15-16 (shared commentary)

### Translation
