This is why the Messenger of God ﷺ circumambulated behind al-Hijr, and informed that al-Hijr is part of the House, and did not touch the two Syrian corners, because they were not completed according to the ancient foundations of Ibrahim (peace be upon him). This is why Ibn Abi Hatim said:

[chain] Ibn Abbas said: When this verse was revealed, {And let them circumambulate the Ancient House}, the Messenger of God ﷺ circumambulated from behind it.

Qatada reported from al-Hasan al-Basri concerning His saying, {And let them circumambulate the Ancient House}: [he said] because it is the first House established for mankind. Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said likewise.

From Ikrima, he said: it was only named "the Ancient House" (al-Bayt al-Atiq) because it was freed (u'tiqa) on the day of the Flood, in the time of Nuh (peace be upon him).

Khusayf said: it was only named al-Bayt al-Atiq because no tyrant ever prevailed over it.

Ibn Abi Najih and Layth reported from Mujahid: it was freed from the tyrants, meaning they were never given power over it. Qatada said likewise.

Hammad ibn Salama reported from Humayd, from al-Hasan ibn Muslim, from Mujahid: because no one ever intended it harm without perishing.

Abd al-Razzaq reported from Ma'mar, from al-Zuhri, from Ibn al-Zubayr, who said: it was only named al-Bayt al-Atiq because God freed it from the tyrants.

Al-Tirmidhi said: [chain] Abdullah ibn al-Zubayr said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "It was only named al-Bayt al-Atiq because no tyrant ever prevailed over it."

Ibn Jarir likewise narrated it from Muhammad ibn Sahl al-Najjari, from Abdullah ibn Salih, with the same chain, and said: "if it is authentic." Al-Tirmidhi said: this is a hasan gharib (sound but singularly narrated) hadith. Then he narrated it by another route from al-Zuhri, as a mursal (report with a missing Companion link).

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿لِيَشْهَدُوا مَنَافِعَ لَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: مَنَافِعُ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ؛ أَمَّا مَنَافِعُ الْآخِرَةِ فَرِضْوَانُ اللَّهِ، وَأَمَّا مَنَافِعُ الدُّنْيَا فَمَا يُصِيبُونَ مِنْ مَنَافِعِ البُدْن وَالرِّبْحِ وَالتِّجَارَاتِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: إِنَّهَا مَنَافِعُ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَيْكُمْ جُنَاحٌ أَنْ تَبْتَغُوا فَضْلا مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ﴾ [البقرة: ١٩٨] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَيَذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ [فِي أَيَّامٍ مَعْلُومَاتٍ] عَلَى مَا رَزَقَهُمْ مِنْ بَهِيمَةِ الأنْعَامِ﴾ قَالَ شُعْبَةُ [وهُشَيْم] عَنْ [أَبِي بِشْرٍ عَنْ سَعِيدٍ] عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْأَيْامُ الْمَعْلُومَاتُ: أَيْامُ الْعَشْرِ، وَعَلَّقَهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْهُ بِصِيغَةِ الْجَزْمِ بِهِ . وَيُرْوَى مِثْلُهُ عَنِ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَعَطَاءٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَقَتَادَةِ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وَعَطَاءٍ الْخُرَاسَانِيِّ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمِ النَّخعي. وَهُوَ مَذْهَبُ الشَّافِعِيِّ، وَالْمَشْهُورُ عَنِ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَرْعَرَة، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنْ مُسْلِمٍ البَطِين، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا الْعَمَلُ فِي أَيْامٍ أَفْضَلَ مِنْهَا فِي هَذِهِ" قَالُوا: وَلَا الْجِهَادُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "وَلَا الْجِهَادُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، إِلَّا رَجُلٌ، يَخْرُجُ يُخَاطِرُ بِنَفْسِهِ وَمَالِهِ فَلَمْ يَرْجِعْ بِشَيْءٍ".

وَرَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ . وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ صَحِيحٌ. وَفِي الْبَابِ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، وَأَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، وَعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو، وَجَابِرٍ.

قُلْتُ: وَقَدْ تَقَصَّيْتُ هَذِهِ الطُّرُقَ، وَأَفْرَدْتُ لَهَا جُزْءًا عَلَى حِدَتِهِ ، فَمِنْ ذَلِكَ مَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَفَّان، أَنْبَأَنَا أَبُو عَوَانة، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي زِيَادٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم: "ما مِنْ أَيْامٍ أَعْظَمَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَلَا أَحَبَّ إِلَيْهِ العملُ فِيهِنَّ، مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأَيْامِ الْعَشْرِ، فَأَكْثِرُوا فِيهِمْ مِنَ التَّهْلِيلِ وَالتَّكْبِيرِ وَالتَّحْمِيدِ" وَرُوِيَ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، بِنَحْوِهِ . وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: وَكَانَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ، وَأَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ يَخْرُجَانِ إِلَى السُّوقِ فِي أَيْامِ الْعَشْرِ، فَيُكَبِّرَانِ وَيُكَبِّرُ النَّاسُ بِتَكْبِيرِهِمَا .

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَحْمَدُ عَنْ جَابِرٍ مَرْفُوعًا: إِنَّ هَذَا هُوَ الْعَشْرُ الَّذِي أَقْسَمَ اللَّهُ بِهِ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالْفَجْرِ وَلَيَالٍ عَشْرٍ﴾ [الْفَجْرِ: ١، ٢] .

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: إِنَّهُ الْمُرَادُ بِقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَأَتْمَمْنَاهَا بِعَشْرٍ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٤٢] .

وَفِي سُنَنِ أَبِي دَاوُدَ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ يَصُومُ هَذَا الْعَشْرَ .

وَهَذَا الْعَشْرُ مُشْتَمِلٌ عَلَى يَوْمِ عَرَفَةَ الَّذِي ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ عَنِ أَبِي قَتَادَةَ قَالَ: سُئِلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ عَنْ صِيَامِ يَوْمِ عَرَفَةَ، فَقَالَ: "أَحْتَسِبْ عَلَى اللَّهِ أَنْ يُكَفِّرَ السَّنَةَ الْمَاضِيَةَ وَالْآتِيَةَ" .

وَيَشْتَمِلُ عَلَى يَوْمِ النَّحْرِ الَّذِي هُوَ يَوْمُ الْحَجِّ الْأَكْبَرِ، وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي حَدِيثٍ أَنَّهُ أَفْضَلُ الْأَيْامِ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ .

وَبِالْجُمْلَةِ، فَهَذَا الْعَشْرُ قَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّهُ أَفْضَلُ أَيْامِ السَّنَةِ، كَمَا نَطَقَ بِهِ الْحَدِيثُ، فَفَضَّلَهُ كَثِيرٌ عَلَى عَشْرِ رَمَضَانَ الْأَخِيرِ؛ لِأَنَّ هَذَا يُشْرَعُ فِيهِ مَا يُشْرَعُ فِي ذَلِكَ، مِنْ صِيَامٍ وَصَلَاةٍ وَصَدَقَةٍ وَغَيْرِهِ، وَيَمْتَازُ هَذَا بِاخْتِصَاصِهِ بِأَدَاءِ فَرْضَ الْحَجِّ فِيهِ.

وَقِيلَ: ذَاكَ أَفْضَلُ لِاشْتِمَالِهِ عَلَى لَيْلَةِ الْقَدْرِ، الَّتِي هِيَ خَيْرٌ مِنْ أَلْفِ شَهْرٍ.

وَتَوَسَّطَ آخَرُونَ فَقَالُوا: أَيْامُ هَذَا أَفْضَلُ، وَلَيَالِي ذَاكَ أَفْضَلُ. وَبِهَذَا يَجْتَمِعُ شَمْلُ الْأَدِلَّةِ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

قَوْلٌ ثَانٍ فِي الْأَيْامِ الْمَعْلُومَاتِ: قَالَ الْحَكَمُ، عَنْ مِقْسَم، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْأَيْامُ الْمَعْلُومَاتُ: يَوْمُ النَّحْرِ وَثَلَاثَةُ أَيْامٍ بَعْدَهُ. وَيُرْوَى هَذَا عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمَ النَّخَعي، وَإِلَيْهِ ذَهَبَ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ فِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ.

قَوْلٌ ثَالِثٌ: قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا علي بن الْمَدِينِيِّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عَجْلان، حَدَّثَنِي نَافِعٌ؛ أَنَّ ابْنَ عُمَرَ كَانَ يَقُولُ: الْأَيْامُ الْمَعْلُومَاتُ وَالْمَعْدُودَاتُ هُنَّ جَمِيعُهُنَّ أَرْبَعَةُ أَيْامٍ، فَالْأَيْامُ الْمَعْلُومَاتُ يَوْمُ النَّحْرِ وَيَوْمَانِ بَعْدَهُ، وَالْأَيْامُ الْمَعْدُودَاتُ ثَلَاثَةُ أَيْامِ يَوْمِ النَّحْرِ.

هَذَا إِسْنَادٌ صَحِيحٌ إِلَيْهِ، وَقَالَهُ السُّدِّيُّ: وَهُوَ مَذْهَبُ الْإِمَامِ مَالِكِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ، وَيُعَضِّدُ هَذَا الْقَوْلَ وَالَّذِي قَبْلَهُ قَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿عَلَى مَا رَزَقَهُمْ مِنْ بَهِيمَةِ الأنْعَامِ﴾ يَعْنِي بِهِ: ذِكْرَ اللَّهِ عِنْدَ ذَبْحِهَا.

قَوْلٌ رَابِعٌ: إِنَّهَا يَوْمُ عَرَفَةَ، وَيَوْمُ النَّحْرِ، وَيَوْمٌ آخَرُ بَعْدَهُ. وَهُوَ مَذْهَبُ أَبِي حَنِيفَةَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ وَهْبٍ: حَدَّثَنِي ابْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنِ أَبِيهِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: الْمَعْلُومَاتُ يَوْمُ عَرَفَةَ، وَيَوْمُ النَّحْرِ، وَأَيْامُ التَّشْرِيقِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿عَلَى مَا رَزَقَهُمْ مِنْ بَهِيمَةِ الأنْعَامِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْإِبِلَ وَالْبَقَرَ وَالْغَنَمَ، كَمَا فَصَّلَهَا تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ الْأَنْعَامِ وَأَنَّهَا ﴿ثَمَانِيَةَ أَزْوَاجٍ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ١٤٣] .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا وَأَطْعِمُوا الْبَائِسَ الْفَقِيرَ﴾ اسْتَدَلَّ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ مَنْ ذَهَبَ إِلَى وُجُوبِ الْأَكْلِ مِنَ الْأَضَاحِيِّ وَهُوَ قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ، وَالَّذِي عَلَيْهِ الْأَكْثَرُونَ أَنَّهُ مِنْ بَابِ الرُّخْصَةِ أَوِ الِاسْتِحْبَابِ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَمَّا نَحَرَ هَدْيَهُ أَمَرَ مِنْ كُلِّ بَدَنَةٍ بِبَضْعَةٍ فَتُطْبَخُ، فَأَكَلَ مِنْ لَحْمِهَا، وَحَسَا مِنْ مَرَقِهَا .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ وَهْبٍ: [قَالَ لِي مَالِكٌ: أُحِبُّ أَنْ يَأْكُلَ مِنْ أُضْحِيَّتِهِ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا﴾ : قَالَ ابْنُ وَهْبٍ] وَسَأَلْتُ اللَّيْثَ، فَقَالَ لي مثل ذلك.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا﴾ قَالَ: كَانَ الْمُشْرِكُونَ لَا يَأْكُلُونَ مِنْ ذَبَائِحِهِمْ فَرُخِّصَ لِلْمُسْلِمِينَ، فَمَنْ شَاءَ أَكَلَ، وَمَنْ شَاءَ لَمْ يَأْكُلْ. وَرُوِيَ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَعَطَاءٍ نَحْوُ ذَلِكَ.

قَالَ هُشَيْم، عَنْ حُصَين، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا﴾ : هِيَ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَإِذَا حَلَلْتُمْ فَاصْطَادُوا﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٢] ، ﴿فَإِذَا قُضِيَتِ الصَّلاةُ فَانْتَشِرُوا فِي الأرْضِ﴾ [الْجُمُعَةِ: ١٠] .

وَهَذَا اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ فِي تَفْسِيرِهِ، وَاسْتَدَلَّ مَنْ نَصَرَ الْقَوْلَ بِأَنَّ الْأَضَاحِيَّ يُتَصَدَّقُ مِنْهَا بِالنِّصْفِ بِقَوْلِهِ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا وَأَطْعِمُوا الْبَائِسَ الْفَقِيرَ﴾ ، فَجَزَّأَهَا نِصْفَيْنِ: نِصْفٌ لِلْمُضَحِّي، وَنِصْفٌ لِلْفُقَرَاءِ.

وَالْقَوْلُ الْآخَرُ: أَنَّهَا تُجَزَّأُ ثَلَاثَةَ أَجْزَاءٍ: ثُلُثٌ لَهُ، وَثُلُثٌ يُهْدِيهِ، وَثُلُثٌ يَتَصَدَّقُ بِهِ؛ لِقَوْلِهِ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا وَأَطْعِمُوا الْقَانِعَ وَالْمُعْتَرَّ﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ٣٦] وَسَيَأْتِي الْكَلَامُ عَلَيْهَا عِنْدَهَا، إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ، وَبِهِ الثِّقَةُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿الْبَائِسَ الْفَقِيرَ﴾ ، قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: هُوَ الْمُضْطَرُّ الَّذِي عَلَيْهِ الْبُؤْسُ، [وَالْفَقِيرُ] الْمُتَعَفِّفُ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هُوَ الَّذِي لَا يَبْسُطُ يَدَهُ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: هُوَ الزّمِن. وَقَالَ مُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّانَ: هُوَ الضَّرِيرُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ لْيَقْضُوا تَفَثَهُمْ﴾ : قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هُوَ وَضْعُ [الْإِحْرَامِ] مِنْ حَلْقِ الرَّأْسِ وَلُبْسِ الثِّيَابِ وَقَصِّ الْأَظْفَارِ، وَنَحْوُ ذَلِكَ. وَهَكَذَا رَوَى عَطَاءٌ وَمُجَاهِدٌ، عَنْهُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿ثُمَّ لْيَقْضُوا تَفَثَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: التَّفَثُ: الْمَنَاسِكُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلْيُوفُوا نُذُورَهُمْ﴾ ، قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي: نَحْرَ مَا نَذَرَ مِنْ أَمْرِ البُدن.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَلْيُوفُوا نُذُورَهُمْ﴾ : نَذْرَ الْحَجِّ وَالْهَدْيِ وَمَا نَذَرَ الْإِنْسَانُ مِنْ شَيْءٍ يَكُونُ فِي الْحَجِّ.

وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مَيْسَرَة، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَلْيُوفُوا نُذُورَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ: الذَّبَائِحُ.

وَقَالَ لَيْثُ بْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَلْيُوفُوا نُذُورَهُمْ﴾ كُلُّ نَذْرٍ إِلَى أَجَلٍ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: ﴿وَلْيُوفُوا نُذُورَهُمْ﴾ ، قَالَ: [حَجَّهُمْ.

وَكَذَا رَوَى الْإِمَامُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي عُمَرَ، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلْيُوفُوا نُذُورَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ:] نَذْرَ الْحَجِّ، فَكُلُّ مَنْ دَخَلَ الْحَجَّ فَعَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْعَمَلِ فِيهِ: الطواف بالبيت وَبَيْنَ الصَّفَا وَالْمَرْوَةِ، وَعَرَفَةُ، وَالْمُزْدَلِفَةُ، وَرَمِيُ الْجِمَارِ، عَلَى مَا أُمِرُوا بِهِ. وَرُوِيَ عَنْ مَالِكٍ نَحْوٌ هَذَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلْيَطَّوَّفُوا بِالْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾ : قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَعْنِي: الطَّوَافَ الْوَاجِبَ يَوْمَ النَّحْرِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادٌ، عَنِ أَبِي حَمْزَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ لِي ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَتَقْرَأُ سُورَةُ الْحَجِّ؟ يَقُولُ اللَّهُ: ﴿وَلْيَطَّوَّفُوا بِالْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾ ، فَإِنَّ آخِرَ الْمَنَاسِكِ الطَّوَافُ بِالْبَيْتِ.

قُلْتُ: وَهَكَذَا صَنَعَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَإِنَّهُ لَمَّا رَجَعَ إِلَى مِنَى يَوْمَ النَّحْرِ بَدَأَ يَرْمِي الْجَمْرَةَ، فَرَمَاهَا بِسَبْعِ حَصَيَاتٍ، ثُمَّ نَحَرَ هَدْيَهُ، وَحَلَقَ رَأْسَهُ، ثُمَّ أَفَاضَ فَطَافَ بِالْبَيْتِ. وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: أُمِرَ النَّاسُ أَنْ يَكُونَ آخِرَ عَهْدِهِمْ بِالْبَيْتِ الطَّوَافُ، إِلَّا أَنَّهُ خُفِّفَ عَنِ الْمَرْأَةِ الْحَائِضِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿بِالْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾ : فِيهِ مُسْتَدَلٌّ لِمَنْ ذَهَبَ إِلَى أَنَّهُ يَجِبُ الطَّوَافُ مِنْ وَرَاءِ الْحِجْرِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ مِنْ أَصْلِ الْبَيْتِ الَّذِي بَنَاهُ إِبْرَاهِيمُ، وَإِنْ كَانَتْ قُرَيْشٌ قَدْ أَخْرَجُوهُ مِنَ الْبَيْتِ، حِينَ قَصُرَتْ بِهِمُ النَّفَقَةُ؛ وَلِهَذَا طَافَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنْ وَرَاءِ الحِجْر، وَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّ الْحِجْرَ مِنَ الْبَيْتِ، وَلَمْ يَسْتَلِمِ الرُّكْنَيْنِ الشَّامِيَّيْنِ؛ لِأَنَّهُمَا لَمْ يُتَمَّمَا عَلَى قَوَاعِدِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْعَتِيقَةِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ:

حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ أَبِي عُمَرَ العَدَني، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ حُجْر، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ: ﴿وَلْيَطَّوَّفُوا بِالْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾ ، طَافَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ من وَرَائِهِ .

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلْيَطَّوَّفُوا بِالْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾ [قَالَ] : لِأَنَّهُ أَوَّلُ بَيْتٍ وُضِعَ لِلنَّاسِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ.

وَعَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ الْبَيْتَ الْعَتِيقَ؛ لِأَنَّهُ أُعْتِقَ يَوْمَ الْغَرَقِ زَمَانَ نُوحٍ.

وَقَالَ خَصِيف: إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ الْبَيْتَ الْعَتِيقَ؛ لِأَنَّهُ لَمْ يَظْهَرْ عَلَيْهِ جَبَّارٌ قَطُّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح وَلَيْثٌ عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: أُعْتِقَ مِنَ الْجَبَابِرَةِ أَنْ يُسَلَّطُوا عَلَيْهِ. وَكَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ.

وَقَالَ حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ حُمَيْدٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: لِأَنَّهُ لَمْ يُرِده أَحَدٌ بِسُوءٍ إِلَّا هَلَكَ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ قَالَ: إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ الْبَيْتَ الْعَتِيقَ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ أَعْتَقَهُ مِنَ الْجَبَابِرَةِ .

وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ صَالِحٍ، أخبرني اللَّيْثُ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ خَالِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ شِهَابٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عُرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الزُّبَيْرِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ الْبَيْتَ الْعَتِيقَ؛ لِأَنَّهُ لَمْ يَظْهَرْ عَلَيْهِ جَبَّارٌ".

وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ سَهْلٍ النَّجَّارِيِّ ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ صَالِحٍ، بِهِ . وَقَالَ: إِنْ كَانَ صَحِيحًا وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ، ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، مُرْسَلًا .

---

## 22:30-31 — verses 30-31 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted says: this is what We have commanded of acts of obedience in the performance of the rites, and what great reward there is for the one who does them.

{And whoever magnifies the sacred things of Allah}, that is: whoever avoids His acts of disobedience and His forbidden things, and regards committing them as something grave in his own soul, {it is better for him with his Lord}, that is: for that he shall have abundant good and generous reward. For just as there is generous reward and great recompense for performing acts of obedience, likewise there is reward for abandoning the forbidden things and avoiding the prohibited matters.

Ibn Jurayj said: Mujahid said concerning His statement, {That, and whoever magnifies the sacred things of Allah}: the sacred thing (al-hurma) is Mecca, the Hajj, and the Umrah, and everything that Allah has forbidden of His acts of disobedience altogether. Ibn Zayd said the same.

And His statement, {And the cattle have been made lawful for you, except that which is recited to you}, that is: We have made lawful for you all the cattle, and what Allah did not designate as a bahirah, nor a sa'ibah, nor a wasilah, nor a ham.

And His statement, {except that which is recited to you}, that is, from the prohibition of {carrion, blood, the flesh of swine, that which has been dedicated to other than Allah, the strangled animal, the one beaten to death, the one that falls to its death, the one gored to death, and that which a wild beast has eaten, except what you slaughter} [al-Ma'idah: 3], to the end of the verse. Ibn Jarir said this, and related it from Qatadah.

And His statement, {So avoid the abomination of idols, and avoid false speech}: "min" here is for clarifying the genus, that is: avoid the abomination which consists of idols. He joined associating partners with Allah together with false speech, just as in His statement: {Say, my Lord has only forbidden indecencies, what is apparent of them and what is concealed, and sin, and wrongful transgression, and that you associate with Allah that for which He has not sent down any authority, and that you say about Allah that which you do not know} [al-A'raf: 33]. False testimony belongs to this category. In the two Sahihs, from Abu Bakrah, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Shall I not inform you of the greatest of the major sins?" We said, "Yes, O Messenger of Allah." He said, "Associating partners with Allah, and disobedience to one's parents." He had been reclining, then he sat up and said, "and indeed, false speech, indeed, false testimony." He kept repeating it until we said, "if only he would stop."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Ayman ibn Khuraym said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ stood up delivering a sermon and said, "O people, false testimony has been made equivalent to associating partners with Allah," three times, then he recited: {So avoid the abomination of idols, and avoid false speech}.

Al-Tirmidhi likewise narrated it from Ahmad ibn Mani', from Marwan ibn Mu'awiyah, by this chain, then said: "gharib (singular), we only know it through the hadith of Sufyan ibn Ziyad. There has been disagreement concerning him in the narration of this hadith, and we do not know of Ayman ibn Khuraym having heard directly from the Prophet ﷺ."

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Khuraym ibn Fatik al-Asadi said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ prayed the dawn prayer, and when he finished he stood up and said, "false testimony has been made equivalent to associating partners with Allah, Mighty and Majestic," then he recited this verse: {So avoid the abomination of idols, and avoid false speech, being upright for Allah, not associating partners with Him}.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Asim ibn Abi al-Najud, from Wa'il ibn Rabi'ah, from Ibn Mas'ud, that he said: false testimony is equivalent to associating partners with Allah, then he recited this verse.

And His statement, {being upright for Allah}, that is: being sincere to Him in religion, turning away from falsehood, aiming purposefully toward truth. For this reason He said, {not associating partners with Him}.

Then He struck a parable for the one who associates partners with Allah, concerning his straying, his ruin, and his distance from guidance, saying: {And whoever associates partners with Allah, it is as if he had fallen from the sky}, that is: fallen down from it, {and the birds snatch him away}, that is: the birds tear him apart in the air, {or the wind blows him down into a far off place}, that is: a distant place, destructive for whoever falls into it. For this reason it comes in the hadith of al-Bara': "Indeed when the angels of death take the disbeliever's soul and ascend with his spirit to the sky, the gates of heaven are not opened for him, rather his spirit is cast down forcefully from there." Then he recited this verse. The hadith has already been given in full, with its wording and its chains, in Surat Ibrahim.

Allah, the Exalted, has also struck another parable for the one who associates partners with Him, in Surat al-An'am, which is His statement: {Say, shall we call upon, besides Allah, that which neither benefits us nor harms us, and be turned back on our heels after Allah has guided us, like one whom the devils have lured to wander confused in the earth, having companions who call him to guidance, saying, come to us. Say, indeed the guidance of Allah, it is the guidance, and we have been commanded to submit to the Lord of all the worlds} [al-An'am: 71].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: هَذَا الَّذِي أَمَرْنَا بِهِ مِنَ الطَّاعَاتِ فِي أَدَاءِ الْمَنَاسِكِ، وَمَا لِفَاعِلِهَا مِنَ الثَّوَابِ الْجَزِيلِ.

﴿وَمَنْ يُعَظِّمْ حُرُمَاتِ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: وَمَنْ يَجْتَنِبُ مَعَاصِيَهُ وَمَحَارِمَهُ وَيَكُونُ ارْتِكَابُهَا عَظِيمًا فِي نَفْسِهِ، ﴿فَهُوَ خَيْرٌ لَهُ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِ﴾ أَيْ: فَلَهُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ خَيْرٌ كَثِيرٌ وَثَوَابٌ جَزِيلٌ، فَكَمَا عَلَى فِعْلِ الطَّاعَاتِ ثَوَابٌ جَزِيلٌ وَأَجْرٌ كَبِيرٌ، وَكَذَلِكَ عَلَى تَرْكِ الْمُحَرَّمَاتِ وَ [اجْتِنَابِ] الْمَحْظُورَاتِ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿ذَلِكَ وَمَنْ يُعَظِّمْ حُرُمَاتِ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: الْحُرْمَةُ: مَكَّةُ وَالْحَجُّ وَالْعُمْرَةُ، وَمَا نَهَى اللَّهُ عَنْهُ مِنْ مَعَاصِيهِ كُلِّهَا. وَكَذَا قَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأُحِلَّتْ لَكُمُ الأنْعَامُ إِلا مَا يُتْلَى عَلَيْكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَحْلَلْنَا لَكُمْ جَمِيعَ الْأَنْعَامِ، وَمَا جَعَلَ اللَّهُ مِنْ بَحِيرَةٍ، وَلَا سَائِبَةٍ، وَلَا وَصِيلَةٍ، وَلَا حَامٍ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا مَا يُتْلَى عَلَيْكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ تَحْرِيمِ ﴿الْمَيْتَةُ وَالدَّمُ وَلَحْمُ الْخِنزيرِ وَمَا أُهِلَّ لِغَيْرِ اللَّهِ بِهِ وَالْمُنْخَنِقَةُ وَالْمَوْقُوذَةُ وَالْمُتَرَدِّيَةُ وَالنَّطِيحَةُ وَمَا أَكَلَ السَّبُعُ [إِلا مَا ذَكَّيْتُمْ] ﴾ الْآيَةَ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٣] ، قَالَ ذَلِكَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وَحَكَاهُ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَاجْتَنِبُوا الرِّجْسَ مِنَ الأوْثَانِ وَاجْتَنِبُوا قَوْلَ الزُّورِ﴾ : "مِنْ" هَاهُنَا لِبَيَانِ الْجِنْسِ، أَيِ: اجْتَنِبُوا الرِّجْسَ الَّذِي هُوَ الْأَوْثَانُ. وَقَرَنَ الشِّرْكَ بِاللَّهِ بِقَوْلِ الزُّورِ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿قُلْ إِنَّمَا حَرَّمَ رَبِّيَ الْفَوَاحِشَ مَا ظَهَرَ مِنْهَا وَمَا بَطَنَ وَالإثْمَ وَالْبَغْيَ بِغَيْرِ الْحَقِّ وَأَنْ تُشْرِكُوا بِاللَّهِ مَا لَمْ يُنزلْ بِهِ سُلْطَانًا وَأَنْ تَقُولُوا عَلَى اللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعْلَمُونَ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ٣٣] ، وَمِنْهُ شَهَادَةُ الزُّورِ. وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنِ أَبِي بَكْرَة قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَلَا أُنْبِئُكُمْ بِأَكْبَرِ الْكَبَائِرِ؟ " قُلْنَا: بَلَى، يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ. قَالَ: "الْإِشْرَاكُ بِاللَّهِ وَعُقُوقُ الْوَالِدَيْنِ -وَكَانَ مُتَّكِئًا فَجَلَسَ، فَقَالَ:-أَلَا وَقَوْلُ الزُّورِ، أَلَا وَشَهَادَةُ الزُّورِ". فَمَا زَالَ يُكَرِّرُهَا، حَتَّى قُلْنَا: لَيْتَهُ سكت .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مَرْوَانُ بْنُ مُعَاوِيَةَ الْفَزَارِيُّ، أَنْبَأَنَا سُفْيَانُ بْنُ زِيَادٍ، عَنْ فَاتِكِ بْنِ فَضَالَةَ، عَنْ أَيْمَنَ بْنِ خُرَيْمٍ قَالَ: قَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ خَطِيبًا فَقَالَ: "يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ، عَدَلَتْ شَهَادَةُ الزُّورِ إِشْرَاكًا بِاللَّهِ" ثَلَاثًا، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿فَاجْتَنِبُوا الرِّجْسَ مِنَ الأوْثَانِ وَاجْتَنِبُوا قَوْلَ الزُّورِ﴾

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ، عَنْ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ مَنِيعٍ، عَنْ مَرْوَانَ بْنِ مُعَاوِيَةَ، بِهِ ثُمَّ قَالَ: "غَرِيبٌ، إِنَّمَا نَعْرِفُهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ زِيَادٍ. وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ عَنْهُ فِي رِوَايَةِ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ، وَلَا نَعْرِفُ لِأَيْمَنَ بْنِ خُرَيْمٍ سَمَاعًا مِنَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ".

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُبَيْدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سفيان العُصْفُرِيّ، عن أبيه، عن حبيب ابن النُّعْمَانِ الْأَسَدِيِّ، عَنْ خُرَيْمِ بْنِ فَاتَكٍ الْأَسَدِيِّ قَالَ: صَلَّى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ الصُّبْحَ، فَلَمَّا انْصَرَفَ قَامَ قَائِمًا فَقَالَ: "عَدَلَتْ شَهَادَةُ الزُّورِ الْإِشْرَاكَ بِاللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ"، ثُمَّ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿فَاجْتَنِبُوا الرِّجْسَ مِنَ الأوْثَانِ وَاجْتَنِبُوا قَوْلَ الزُّورِ حُنَفَاءَ لِلَّهِ غَيْرَ مُشْرِكِينَ بِهِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ عَاصِمِ بْنِ أَبِي النَّجُودِ، عَنْ وَائِلِ بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: تَعْدِلُ شَهَادَةُ الزُّورِ بِالشِّرْكِ بِاللَّهِ، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿حُنَفَاءَ لِلَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: مُخْلِصِينَ لَهُ الدِّينَ، مُنْحَرِفِينَ عَنِ الْبَاطِلِ قَصْدًا إِلَى الْحَقِّ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ ﴿غَيْرَ مُشْرِكِينَ بِهِ﴾

ثُمَّ ضَرَبَ لِلْمُشْرِكِ مَثَلًا فِي ضَلَالِهِ وَهَلَاكِهِ وَبُعْدِهِ عَنِ الْهُدَى فَقَالَ: ﴿وَمَنْ يُشْرِكْ بِاللَّهِ فَكَأَنَّمَا خَرَّ مِنَ السَّمَاءِ﴾ أَيْ: سَقَطَ مِنْهَا، ﴿فَتَخْطَفُهُ الطَّيْرُ﴾ ، أَيْ: تَقْطَعُهُ الطُّيُورُ فِي الْهَوَاءِ، ﴿أَوْ تَهْوِي بِهِ الرِّيحُ فِي مَكَانٍ سَحِيقٍ﴾ أَيْ: بَعِيدٍ مُهْلِكٍ لِمَنْ هَوَى فِيهِ؛ وَلِهَذَا جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثِ الْبَرَاءِ: "إِنَّ الْكَافِرَ إِذَا تَوَفَّتْهُ مَلَائِكَةُ الْمَوْتِ، وَصَعِدُوا بِرُوحِهِ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ، فَلَا تُفْتَحُ لَهُ أَبْوَابُ السَّمَاءِ، بَلْ تُطْرَحُ رُوحُهُ طَرْحًا مِنْ هُنَاكَ". ثُمَّ قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ، وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْحَدِيثُ فِي سُورَةِ "إِبْرَاهِيمَ" بِحُرُوفِهِ وَأَلْفَاظِهِ وَطُرُقِهِ.

وَقَدْ ضَرَبَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى لِلْمُشْرِكِ مَثَلًا آخَرَ فِي سُورَةِ "الْأَنْعَامِ"، وَهُوَ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿قُلْ أَنَدْعُو مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يَنْفَعُنَا وَلا يَضُرُّنَا وَنُرَدُّ عَلَى أَعْقَابِنَا بَعْدَ إِذْ هَدَانَا اللَّهُ كَالَّذِي اسْتَهْوَتْهُ الشَّيَاطِينُ فِي الأرْضِ حَيْرَانَ لَهُ أَصْحَابٌ يَدْعُونَهُ إِلَى الْهُدَى ائْتِنَا قُلْ إِنَّ هُدَى اللَّهِ هُوَ الْهُدَى [وَأُمِرْنَا لِنُسْلِمَ لِرَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ] ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ: ٧١] .

---

## 22:32-33 — verses 32-33 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, this: {And whoever honors the symbols (sha'a'ir) of Allah}, meaning His commands, {indeed it is from the piety of hearts}. Among this is the honoring of sacrificial offerings and camels designated for sacrifice, as al-Hakam said, from Miqsam, from Ibn Abbas: honoring them means making them plump and choosing them well.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Abu Sa'id al-Ashajj narrated to us, Hafs ibn Ghiyath narrated to us, from Ibn Abi Layla, from Ibn Abi Najih, from Mujahid, from Ibn Abbas, regarding {That, and whoever honors the symbols of Allah}: he said, it means making them plump, choosing them well, and holding them in high regard.

Abu Umamah ibn Sahl said: We used to fatten the sacrificial animal in Medina, and the Muslims used to fatten them. Related by al-Bukhari.

From Abu Hurayrah, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The blood of a pale-colored animal is more beloved to Allah than the blood of two black ones." Related by Ahmad and Ibn Majah.

They said: al-'afra' is the one whose whiteness is not pure white. So the white one is superior to others, though others are also sufficient, because of what is established in Sahih al-Bukhari from Anas: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ sacrificed two horned rams that were piebald (white mixed with black).

From Abu Sa'id: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ sacrificed a horned, virile ram that ate from black, looked from black, and walked in black.

Related by the compilers of the Sunan, and authenticated by al-Tirmidhi, meaning: a black ram in these places (around the eyes, mouth, and legs).

In the Sunan of Ibn Majah, from Abu Rafi': that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ sacrificed two large, fat, horned, piebald rams that were mawju'ayn. It was said: these two were castrated. It was also said: these were ones whose testicles had been crushed but not cut off. And Allah knows best.

Likewise, Abu Dawud and Ibn Majah related from Jabir: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ sacrificed two horned, piebald rams that were mawju'ayn (the mawju'ayn were said to be the castrated ones).

From Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded us to examine closely the eye and the ear, and that we should not sacrifice an animal that is muqabalah, mudabarah, sharqa', or kharqa'.

Related by Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan, and authenticated by al-Tirmidhi.

And they also related from him, he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ forbade that we sacrifice an animal with a broken horn or ear (a'dab al-qarn wal-udhn).

Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab said: al-'adb means half or more (of the horn or ear broken off).

Some scholars of language said: if the upper part of its horn is broken, it is qasma'; as for al-'adb, it is the breaking of the lower part, and 'adb of the ear is the cutting off of part of it.

According to al-Shafi'i, sacrificing such an animal is sufficient, but disliked.

Imam Ahmad said: The sacrifice of an animal with a broken horn or ear is not sufficient, on account of this hadith.

Malik said: if blood flows from the horn, it is not sufficient; otherwise it is sufficient. And Allah knows best.

As for al-muqabalah: it is the one whose front part of the ear has been cut off. Al-mudabarah: from the back part of its ear. Al-sharqa': it is the one whose ear has been slit lengthwise, as said by al-Shafi'i. Al-kharqa': it is the one whose ear has a round hole torn in it as a mark. And Allah knows best.

From al-Bara', he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Four are not permissible in sacrificial animals: the one-eyed whose blindness is clearly evident, the sick one whose sickness is clearly evident, the lame one whose limping is clearly evident, and the emaciated one that has no marrow left."

Related by Ahmad and the compilers of the Sunan, and authenticated by al-Tirmidhi.

These defects diminish the meat, due to the animal's weakness and inability to graze fully, because the other sheep outpace it to the pasture. For this reason, sacrifice with such an animal is not sufficient according to al-Shafi'i and other imams, as is apparent from the hadith.

Al-Shafi'i's position differed regarding an animal with a minor sickness, giving two views.

Abu Dawud related, from 'Utbah ibn 'Abd al-Sulami, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ forbade al-musaffarah, al-musta'salah, al-bakhqa', al-mushayya'ah, and al-kasra'.

Al-musaffarah was said to mean: the emaciated one. It was also said: the one whose ear is entirely cut off. Al-musta'salah: the one whose horn is broken off. Al-bakhqa': the one-eyed. Al-mushayya'ah: the one that always has to be driven along behind the flock and cannot keep up on its own due to its weakness. Al-kasra': the lame one.

All these defects prevent the sacrifice from being sufficient. But if the defect occurs after the animal has been designated as the sacrifice, then its defect does not cause harm according to al-Shafi'i, unlike Abu Hanifah's view.

Imam Ahmad related, from Abu Sa'id, he said: I bought a ram to sacrifice, and a wolf ran off and took its fat tail. So I asked the Prophet ﷺ, and he said: "Sacrifice it." For this reason it came in the hadith: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded us to examine closely the eye and the ear. That is, that the sacrificial offering or the sacrifice should be fat, good, and valuable, as related by Imam Ahmad and Abu Dawud, from Abdullah ibn Umar, he said: Umar offered a fine she-camel as a sacrificial gift, and was offered three hundred dinars for it. So he came to the Prophet ﷺ and said: O Messenger of Allah, I offered a fine she-camel as a sacrificial gift, and I was offered three hundred dinars for it. Shall I sell it and buy with its price several camels? He said: "No, sacrifice it as it is."

Al-Dahhak said, from Ibn Abbas: the sacrificial camels (al-budn) are among the symbols of Allah.

Muhammad ibn Abi Musa said: standing at Arafat, Muzdalifah, the pillars, the throwing of pebbles, the sacrificial camels, and the shaving of the head are all among the symbols of Allah.

Ibn Umar said: the greatest of the symbols is the House (the Ka'bah).

His saying: {For you in them are benefits}, meaning: for you there are benefits in the sacrificial camels, from their milk, their wool, their fur, their hair, and riding upon them.

{Until a specified term}: Miqsam said, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His saying: {For you in them are benefits until a specified term}, he said: it means as long as it has not been designated as a sacrificial camel.

Mujahid said, regarding His saying {For you in them are benefits until a specified term}: he said: riding, milk, and offspring; but once it has been designated as a badanah (sacrificial camel) or hady (sacrificial offering), all of that ceases. Likewise said 'Ata', al-Dahhak, Qatadah, Muqatil, 'Ata' al-Khurasani, and others.

Others said: rather, one may benefit from it even if it has been designated as a hady, if there is need for that, as is established in the two Sahihs from Anas: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ saw a man driving a sacrificial camel, and said: "Ride it." The man said: it is a sacrificial camel (badanah). He said: "Ride it, woe to you," the second or third time.

In a narration of Muslim, from Jabir, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "Ride it in a reasonable manner when you are compelled to it."

Shu'bah said, from Zuhayr ibn Abi Thabit al-A'ma, from al-Mughirah ibn Hadhf, from Ali: that he saw a man driving a sacrificial camel with its young alongside it, and he said: do not drink from its milk except what is surplus to the needs of its young, and when the Day of Sacrifice comes, slaughter it and its young.

His saying: {Then its place of sacrifice is at the Ancient House}, meaning: the place where the sacrificial offering is completed and its final destination is at the Ancient House, which is the Ka'bah, as the Almighty says: {a sacrificial offering reaching the Ka'bah} [al-Ma'idah: 95], and He says: {and the sacrificial animals held back, prevented from reaching their place of sacrifice} [al-Fath: 25].

Discussion of the meaning of "the Ancient House" has already preceded shortly before, and praise be to Allah.

Ibn Jurayj said, from 'Ata': Ibn Abbas used to say: whoever has performed the circumambulation (tawaf) of the House has thereby become released from the state of ihram. Allah the Almighty says: {then its place of sacrifice is at the Ancient House}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: هَذَا ﴿وَمَنْ يُعَظِّمْ شَعَائِرَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ: أَوَامِرَهُ، ﴿فَإِنَّهَا مِنْ تَقْوَى الْقُلُوبِ﴾ وَمِنْ ذَلِكَ تَعْظِيمُ الْهَدَايَا وَالْبُدْنِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْحَكَمُ، عَنْ مقْسَم، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: تَعْظِيمُهَا: اسْتِسْمَانُهَا وَاسْتِحْسَانُهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو سعيد الأشج، حَدَّثَنَا حَفْصُ بْنُ غِيَاثٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿ذَلِكَ وَمَنْ يُعَظِّمْ شَعَائِرَ اللَّهِ﴾ قَالَ: الِاسْتِسْمَانُ وَالِاسْتِحْسَانُ وَالِاسْتِعْظَامُ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو أُمَامَةَ بْنُ سَهْلٍ: كُنَّا نُسَمِّنُ الْأُضْحِيَّةَ بِالْمَدِينَةِ، وَكَانَ الْمُسْلِمُونَ يُسمّنون. رَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ .

وَعَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "دَمُ عفراءَ أَحَبُّ إِلَى اللَّهِ مِنْ دَمِ سَوداوين". رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ .

قَالُوا: وَالْعَفْرَاءُ هِيَ الْبَيْضَاءُ بَيَاضًا لَيْسَ بِنَاصِعٍ، فَالْبَيْضَاءُ أَفْضَلُ مِنْ غَيْرِهَا، وَغَيْرُهَا يُجْزِئُ أَيْضًا؛ لِمَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ ضَحَّى بِكَبْشَيْنِ أَمْلَحَيْنِ أَقْرَنَيْنِ .

وَعَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ ضَحَّى بِكَبْشٍ أَقْرَنَ فَحيل يَأْكُلُ فِي سَوَادٍ، وَيَنْظُرُ فِي سَوَادٍ، وَيَمْشِي فِي سَوَادٍ.

رَوَاهُ أَهْلُ السُّنَنِ، وَصَحَّحَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ ، أَيْ: بِكَبْشٍ أَسْوَدَ فِي هَذِهِ الْأَمَاكِنِ.

وَفِي سُنَنِ ابْنِ مَاجَهْ، عَنْ أَبِي رَافِعٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ ضَحَّى بِكَبْشَيْنِ عَظِيمَيْنِ سَمِينَيْنِ أَقْرَنَيْنِ أَمْلَحَيْنِ مَوْجُوءَيْنِ . قِيلَ: هُمَا الخَصِيَان. وَقِيلَ: اللَّذَانِ رُضَّ خُصْياهما، وَلَمْ يَقْطَعْهُمَا ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَكَذَا رَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ عَنْ جَابِرٍ: ضَحَّى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِكَبْشَيْنِ أَقْرَنَيْنِ أَمْلَحَيْنِ مَوْجُوءَيْنِ [والموجوءين قيل: هما الخصيين] .

وَعَنْ عَلِيٍّ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: أَمَرَنَا رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إن نَسْتَشْرِفَ الْعَيْنَ وَالْأُذُنَ، وَأَلَّا نُضَحِّيَ بمقابَلَة، وَلَا مدابَرَة، وَلَا شَرْقاء، وَلَا خَرْقاء.

رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ، وَصَحَّحَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ .

وَلَهُمْ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: نَهَى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إن نُضحي بأعضب القرن والأذن .

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ الْمُسَيَّبِ: الْعَضْبُ: النصْف فَأَكْثَرُ.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُ أَهْلِ اللُّغَةِ: إِنْ كُسر قَرْنُهَا الْأَعْلَى فَهِيَ قَصْمَاءُ، فَأَمَّا العَضْب فَهُوَ كَسْرُ الْأَسْفَلِ، وَعَضَبُ الْأُذُنِ قَطْعُ بَعْضِهَا.

وَعِنْدَ الشَّافِعِيِّ أَنَّ التَّضْحِيَةَ بِذَلِكَ مُجْزِئَةٌ، لَكِنْ تُكْرَهُ.

وَقَالَ [الْإِمَامُ] أَحْمَدُ: لَا تُجْزِئُ الْأُضْحِيَّةُ بِأَعْضَبِ الْقَرْنِ وَالْأُذُنِ؛ لِهَذَا الْحَدِيثِ.

وَقَالَ مَالِكٌ: إِنْ كَانَ الدَّمُ يَسِيلُ مِنَ الْقَرْنِ لَمْ يُجَزِئْ، وَإِلَّا أَجَزَأَ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَأَمَّا الْمُقَابَلَةُ: فَهِيَ الَّتِي قُطِعَ مُقَدَّمُ أُذُنِهَا، وَالْمُدَابَرَةُ: مِنْ مُؤَخَّرِ أُذُنِهَا. وَالشَّرْقَاءُ: هِيَ الَّتِي قُطِعَتْ أُذُنُهَا طُولًا قَالَهُ الشَّافِعِيُّ. وَالْخَرْقَاءُ: هِيَ الَّتِي خَرَقت السّمَةُ أُذُنُهَا خَرْقًا مُدَوّرًا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَعَنِ الْبَرَاءِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "أَرْبَعٌ لَا تَجُوزُ فِي الْأَضَاحِي: الْعَوْرَاءُ الْبَيِّنُ عَوَرها، وَالْمَرِيضَةُ الْبَيِّنُ مَرَضها، وَالْعَرْجَاءُ الْبَيِّنُ ظَلَعها ، وَالْكَسِيرَةُ الَّتِي لَا تُنقِي".

رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ، وَصَحَّحَهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ .

وَهَذِهِ الْعُيُوبُ تَنْقُصُ اللَّحْمَ، لِضَعْفِهَا وَعَجْزِهَا عَنِ اسْتِكْمَالِ الرَّعْيِ؛ لِأَنَّ الشَّاءَ يَسْبِقُونَهَا إِلَى الْمَرْعَى، فَلِهَذَا لَا تُجْزِئُ التَّضْحِيَةُ بِهَا عِنْدَ الشَّافِعِيِّ وَغَيْرِهِ مِنَ الْأَئِمَّةِ، كَمَا هُوَ ظَاهِرُ الْحَدِيثِ.

وَاخْتَلَفَ قَوْلُ الشَّافِعِيِّ فِي الْمَرِيضَةِ مَرَضًا يَسِيرًا، عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ.

وَرَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ عُتبة بْنِ عَبْدٍ السّلَمي؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ نَهَى عَنِ المُصْفَرَةِ، والمستأصَلَة، والبَخْقاء، والمشيَّعة، وَالْكَسْرَاءِ .

فَالْمُصْفَرَّةُ قِيلَ: الْهَزِيلَةُ. وَقِيلَ: الْمُسْتَأْصَلَةُ الأذنُ. وَالْمُسْتَأْصَلَةُ: الْمَكْسُورَةُ الْقَرْنِ. وَالْبَخْقَاءُ: هِيَ الْعَوْرَاءُ. وَالْمُشَيَّعَةُ: هِيَ الَّتِي لَا تَزَالُ تُشَيَّع خَلفَ الْغَنَمِ، وَلَا تَتْبَع لِضَعْفِهَا. وَالْكَسْرَاءُ: الْعَرْجَاءُ.

فَهَذِهِ الْعُيُوبُ كُلُّهَا مَانعَةٌ [مِنَ الْإِجْزَاءِ، فَإِنْ طَرَأَ الْعَيْبُ] بَعْدَ تَعْيِينِ الْأُضْحِيَّةِ فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَضُرُّ عَيْبُهُ عِنْدَ الشَّافِعِيِّ خِلَافًا لِأَبِي حَنِيفَةَ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى الإمامُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: اشْتَرَيْتُ كَبْشًا أُضَحِّي بِهِ، فَعَدَا الذِّئْبُ فَأَخَذَ الْأَلْيَةَ. فَسَأَلْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ، فَقَالَ: "ضَحِّ بِهِ" وَلِهَذَا [جَاءَ] فِي الْحَدِيثِ: أَمَرَنَا رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنْ نَسْتَشْرِفَ الْعَيْنَ والأذن. أي: أن تكون الْهَدْيَةُ أَوِ الْأُضْحِيَّةُ سَمِينَةً حَسَنَةً ثَمِينَةً، كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: أَهْدَى عُمَرُ نَجيبًا، فَأُعْطِيَ بِهَا ثَلَاثَمِائَةِ دِينَارٍ، فَأَتَى النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنِّي أَهْدَيْتُ نُجَيْبًا، فأعطِيتُ بِهَا ثَلَاثَمِائَةِ دِينَارٍ، أَفَأَبِيعُهَا وَأَشْتَرِي بِثَمَنِهَا بدْنًا؟ قَالَ: "لَا انحَرْهَا إِيَّاهَا" .

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْبُدْنُ مِنْ شَعَائِرِ اللَّهِ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبِي مُوسَى: الْوُقُوفُ وَمُزْدَلِفَةُ وَالْجِمَارُ وَالرَّمْيُ وَالْبُدْنُ وَالْحَلْقُ: مِنْ شَعَائِرِ اللَّهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عُمَرَ: أَعْظَمُ الشَّعَائِرِ الْبَيْتُ.

قَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ﴾ أَيْ: لَكُمْ فِي الْبُدْنِ مَنَافِعُ، مِنْ لَبَنِهَا، وَصُوفِهَا وَأَوْبَارِهَا وَأَشْعَارِهَا، وَرُكُوبِهَا.

﴿إِلَى أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى﴾ : قَالَ مِقْسَم، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ [فِي قَوْلِهِ] : ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ إِلَى أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى﴾ قَالَ: مَا لَمْ يُسَمَّ بُدْنًا.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ إِلَى أَجَلٍ مُسَمًّى﴾ ، قَالَ: الرُّكُوبُ وَاللَّبَنُ وَالْوَلَدُ، فَإِذَا سُمّيت بَدنَةً أَوْ هَديًا، ذَهَبَ ذَلِكَ كُلُّهُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ عَطَاءٌ، وَالضَّحَّاكُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، [وَمُقَاتِلٌ] وَعَطَاءٌ الْخُرَاسَانِيُّ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلْ لَهُ أَنْ يَنْتَفِعَ بِهَا وَإِنْ كَانَتْ هَدْيًا، إِذَا احْتَاجَ إِلَى ذَلِكَ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَنَسٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ رَأَى رَجُلًا يَسُوقُ بدَنَةً، قَالَ: "ارْكَبْهَا". قَالَ: إِنَّهَا بَدنَة. قَالَ: "ارْكَبْهَا، وَيْحَكَ"، فِي الثَّانيَةِ أَوِ الثَّالِثَةِ .

وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ لِمُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "ارْكَبْهَا بِالْمَعْرُوفِ إِذَا ألجئتَ إِلَيْهَا" .

وَقَالَ شُعْبَةُ، عَنْ زُهَيْرِ بْنِ أَبِي ثَابِتٍ الْأَعْمَى، عَنِ الْمُغِيرَةِ بْنِ حَذْف، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ؛ أَنَّهُ رَأَى رَجُلًا يَسُوقُ بَدَنَةً وَمَعَهَا وَلَدُهَا، فَقَالَ: لَا تَشْرَبْ مِنْ لَبَنِهَا إِلَّا مَا فَضُلَ عَنْ وَلَدِهَا، فَإِذَا كَانَ يَوْمُ النَّحْرِ فَاذْبَحْهَا وولدَها.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿ثُمَّ مَحِلُّهَا إِلَى الْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾ أَيْ: مَحِل الْهَدْيِ وَانتِهَاؤُهُ إِلَى الْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ، وَهُوَ الْكَعْبَةُ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿هَدْيًا بَالِغَ الْكَعْبَةِ﴾ [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٩٥] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَالْهَدْيَ مَعْكُوفًا أَنْ يَبْلُغَ مَحِلَّهُ﴾ [الْفَتْحِ: ٢٥] .

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ الْكَلَامُ عَلَى مَعْنَى "الْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ" قَرِيبًا، وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ: كَانَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ: كُلُّ مَنْ طَافَ بِالْبَيْتِ، فَقَدْ حَلَّ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تعالى: ﴿ثُمَّ مَحِلُّهَا إِلَى الْبَيْتِ الْعَتِيقِ﴾

---

## 22:34-35 — verses 34-35 (shared commentary)

### Translation

He, exalted, informs that the slaughtering of sacrificial rites and the shedding of blood in the name of God has always been prescribed in all the religious communities.

Ali ibn Abi Talha said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas, regarding {And for every nation We appointed a rite of sacrifice}: he said, a festival.

Ikrimah said: a slaughter. Zayd ibn Aslam said concerning His saying, {And for every nation We appointed a rite of sacrifice}, that it refers to Mecca; God never appointed for any nation a rite of sacrifice other than it.

[And His saying]: {that they may mention God's name over the beast cattle He has provided them}, as is established in the two Sahihs on the authority of Anas, who said: two horned, piebald rams were brought to the Messenger of God ﷺ, and he named God over them and said "Allahu akbar," and placed his foot upon their sides.

The Imam Ahmad ibn Hanbal said: Yazid ibn Harun told us, Sallam ibn Miskin informed us, from A'idh Allah al-Mujashi'i, from Abu Dawud (that is, Nufay' ibn al-Harith), from Zayd ibn Arqam, who said: I said, or they said: O Messenger of God, what are these sacrificial animals? He said, "The way of your father Abraham." They said, "What is there for us in it?" He said, "For every hair, a good deed." They said, "And the wool?" He said, "For every hair of the wool, a good deed."

The Imam Abu Abdullah Muhammad ibn Yazid Ibn Majah related it in his Sunan, from the hadith of Sallam ibn Miskin, with the same chain.

And His saying: {So your god is one God, so submit to Him}, meaning: your object of worship is one, even though the laws of the prophets varied and some abrogated others, for all of them call to the worship of God alone, with no partner for Him: {And We sent not before you any messenger except that We revealed to him that there is no god but I, so worship Me} [al-Anbiya: 25]. And for this reason He said: {so submit to Him}, meaning: be sincere and surrender to His judgment and obedience to Him.

{And give good tidings to the mukhbitin (those who are humbly submissive)}: Mujahid said: those who are tranquil at rest. Al-Dahhak and Qatadah said: those who are humble. Al-Suddi said: those who are fearful. Amr ibn Aws said: the mukhbitun are those who do not wrong others, and when wronged, do not seek revenge.

Al-Thawri said, regarding {And give good tidings to the mukhbitin}: he said, those who are tranquil, content with God's decree, submissive to Him.

The best explanation of it is what follows it, namely His saying: {those whose hearts fear when God is mentioned}, meaning: their hearts fear Him, {and those who are patient over what befalls them}, meaning: over calamities.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: By God, you will surely be patient or you will surely perish.

{And those who establish prayer}: the majority read it in the construct form (idafa), the seven canonical reciters and the rest of the ten as well. Ibn al-Sumayfa' read it as "al-muqimina al-salata," in the accusative.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: {wa'l-muqimi al-salah}, and the final nun here is dropped only for the sake of lightening the pronunciation; had it been dropped for the sake of the construct form, the word "prayer" would necessarily be in the genitive, but it is dropped as a matter of lightening, so it is placed in the accusative.

Meaning: those who render to God His due in fulfilling what He has obligated upon them of performing His prescribed duties, {and spend from what We have provided them}, meaning: and they spend what God has given them of good provision upon their families, their slaves, their relatives, their poor, and their needy, and they do good to God's creation while maintaining God's limits. This is the opposite of the characteristics of the hypocrites, for they are the reverse of all of this, as was explained previously in Surat Bara'ah (Repentance) [and to God belongs all praise and favor].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَزَل ذبحُ الْمَنَاسِكِ وإراقةُ الدِّمَاءِ عَلَى اسْمِ اللَّهِ مَشْرُوعًا فِي جَمِيعِ الْمِلَلِ.

قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ أُمَّةٍ جَعَلْنَا مَنْسَكًا﴾ قَالَ: عِيدًا.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ: ذَبَحًا. وَقَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلِكُلِّ أُمَّةٍ جَعَلْنَا مَنْسَكًا﴾ ، إِنَّهَا مَكَّةُ، لَمْ يَجْعَلِ اللَّهُ لِأُمَّةٍ قَطُّ مَنْسَكًا غَيْرَهَا.

[وَقَوْلُهُ] : ﴿لِيَذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَى مَا رَزَقَهُمْ مِنْ بَهِيمَةِ الأنْعَامِ﴾ ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَنَسٍ قَالَ: أَتَى رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِكَبْشَيْنِ أَمْلَحَيْنِ أَقْرَنَيْنِ، فسمَّى وَكَبَّرَ، وَوَضَعَ رِجْلَهُ عَلَى صِفَاحهما .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ هَارُونَ، أَنْبَأَنَا سَلام بْنُ مِسْكِينٍ، عَنْ عَائِذِ اللَّهِ الْمُجَاشِعِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي دَاوُدَ -وَهُوَ نُفَيْع بْنُ الْحَارِثِ-عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَرْقَمَ قَالَ: قُلْتُ -أَوْ: قَالُوا-: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، مَا هَذِهِ الْأَضَاحِيُّ؟ قَالَ: "سُنَّةُ أَبِيكُمْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ". قَالُوا: مَا لَنَا مِنْهَا؟ قَالَ: "بِكُلِّ شَعْرَةٍ حَسَنَةٌ" قَالُوا: فَالصُّوفُ؟ قَالَ: "بِكُلِّ شَعْرَةٍ مِنَ الصُّوفِ حَسَنَةٌ".

وَأَخْرَجَهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ يَزِيدَ ابْنِ مَاجَهْ فِي سُنَنِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَلَّامِ بْنِ مِسْكِينٍ، بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَإِلَهُكُمْ إِلَهٌ وَاحِدٌ فَلَهُ أَسْلِمُوا﴾ أَيْ: مَعْبُودُكُمْ وَاحِدٌ، وَإِنْ تَنوّعَت شَرَائِعُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ ونَسخَ بَعْضُهَا بَعْضًا، فَالْجَمِيعُ يَدْعُونَ إِلَى عِبَادَةِ اللَّهِ وَحْدَهُ، لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلا نُوحِي إِلَيْهِ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَهَ إِلا أَنَا فَاعْبُدُونِ﴾ [الْأَنْبِيَاءِ: ٢٥] . وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَلَهُ أَسْلِمُوا﴾ أَيْ: أَخْلِصُوا وَاسْتَسْلِمُوا لحُكْمه وَطَاعَتِهِ.

﴿وَبَشِّرِ الْمُخْبِتِينَ﴾ : قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: الْمُطْمَئِنِّينَ، وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، وَقَتَادَةُ: الْمُتَوَاضِعِينَ. وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: الْوَجِلِينَ. وَقَالَ عَمْرُو بْنُ أَوْسٍ : الْمُخْبِتُونَ : الَّذِينَ لَا يَظلمون، وَإِذَا ظُلموا لَمْ يَنْتَصِرُوا.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ: ﴿وَبَشِّرِ الْمُخْبِتِينَ﴾ قَالَ: الْمُطْمَئِنِّينَ الرَّاضِينَ بِقَضَاءِ اللَّهِ، الْمُسْتَسْلِمِينَ له.

وَأَحْسَنُ مَا يُفَسَّرُ بِمَا بَعْدَهُ وَهُوَ قَوْلُهُ: ﴿الَّذِينَ إِذَا ذُكِرَ اللَّهُ وَجِلَتْ قُلُوبُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: خَافَتْ مِنْهُ قلوبُهم، ﴿وَالصَّابِرِينَ عَلَى مَا أَصَابَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْمَصَائِبِ.

قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: وَاللَّهِ لَتَصْبِرُنَّ أَوْ لَتَهْلِكُنَّ.

﴿وَالْمُقِيمِي الصَّلاةِ﴾ : قَرَأَ الْجُمْهُورُ بِالْإِضَافَةِ. السبعةَ، وبقيةَ الْعَشْرَةِ أَيْضًا. وَقَرَأَ ابْنُ السَّمَيْقَع: "والمقيمينَ الصَّلَاةَ" بِالنَّصْبِ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: ﴿وَالْمُقِيمِي الصَّلاةِ﴾ ، وَإِنَّمَا حُذِفَتِ النُّونُ هَاهُنَا تَخْفِيفًا، وَلَوْ حُذِفَتْ لِلْإِضَافَةِ لَوَجَبَ خَفْضُ الصَّلَاةِ، وَلَكِنْ عَلَى سَبِيلِ التَّخْفِيفِ فَنُصِبَتْ.

أَيِ: الْمُؤَدِّينَ حَقَّ اللَّهِ فِيمَا أَوْجَبَ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ أَدَاءِ فَرَائِضِهِ، ﴿وَمِمَّا رَزَقْنَاهُمْ يُنْفِقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: وَيُنْفِقُونَ مَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ طَيِّبِ الرِّزْقِ عَلَى أَهْلِيهِمْ وَأَرِقَّائِهِمْ وَقُرَابَاتِهِمْ، وَفُقَرَائِهِمْ وَمَحَاوِيجِهِمْ، وَيُحْسِنُونَ إِلَى خَلْقِ اللَّهِ مَعَ مُحَافَظَتِهِمْ عَلَى حُدُودِ اللَّهِ. وَهَذِهِ بِخِلَافِ صِفَاتِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَإِنَّهُمْ بِالْعَكْسِ مِنْ هَذَا كُلِّهِ، كَمَا تَقَدَّمَ تَفْسِيرُهُ فِي سُورَةِ "بَرَاءَةٌ" [فَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ وَالْمِنَّةُ] .

---

## 22:36 — verse 36

### Translation

The Almighty says, bestowing favor upon His servants regarding what He created for them of the budn (sacrificial camels/cattle), and made them among His shaa'ir (rites/symbols), namely that He made them things to be sent as offerings to His Sacred House. Indeed, they are the best of what is offered [to His Sacred House], as the Almighty says: {Do not violate the sanctity of the symbols of Allah, nor the sacred month, nor the sacrificial animals, nor the garlanded ones [nor those going to the Sacred House seeking bounty from their Lord and His pleasure]} (al-Ma'idah: 2).

Ibn Jurayj said: Ata' said concerning His statement, {And the budn We have made for you among the symbols of Allah}: it means cattle and camels. The same has been reported from Ibn Umar, Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab, and al-Hasan al-Basri. Mujahid said: the budn are only from camels.

I say: as for applying the term badanah to a camel, this is agreed upon. They differed over the validity of applying badanah to a cow, on two views, the more correct of which is that it is applied to it in the Sacred Law, as is established in the hadith.

Then the majority of scholars hold that a badanah suffices for seven people, and a cow suffices for seven, as is established by the hadith recorded by Muslim, from the report of Jabir ibn Abdullah [and others], who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded us to share in the sacrificial animals, the badanah for seven and the cow for seven.

[Ishaq ibn Rahawayh and others said: rather, a cow suffices for seven and a camel for ten.] A hadith to this effect has come in the Musnad of Imam Ahmad, the Sunan of al-Nasa'i, and elsewhere. Allah knows best.

Regarding His statement, {For you in them is good}, meaning: reward in the abode of the Hereafter.

From Sulayman ibn Yazid al-Ka'bi, from Hisham ibn Urwah, from his father, from A'ishah, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "No deed done by the son of Adam on the Day of Sacrifice is more beloved to Allah than the shedding of blood. It will come on the Day of Resurrection with its horns, its hooves, and its hair, and the blood reaches a station with Allah before it touches the ground. So be pleased with it in your hearts." Reported by Ibn Majah and al-Tirmidhi, who deemed it hasan (sound).

Sufyan al-Thawri said: Abu Hatim used to borrow money and drive sacrificial camels along. He was asked, "You borrow money and drive sacrificial camels?" He replied: "I heard Allah say, {For you in them is good}."

From Ibn Abbas, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "No silver has been spent on anything more excellent than a sacrificial animal slaughtered on the day of a festival." Reported by al-Daraqutni in his Sunan.

Mujahid said regarding {For you in them is good}: it means reward and benefits.

Ibrahim al-Nakha'i said: one may ride it and milk it if he has need of it.

Regarding His statement, {So mention the name of Allah over them, standing in rows}: from [al-Muttalib ibn Abdullah ibn Hantab, from] Jabir ibn Abdullah, who said: I prayed the Eid al-Adha prayer with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and when he finished, a ram was brought to him and he slaughtered it, saying: "In the name of Allah, and Allah is greatest. O Allah, this is from me and from whoever among my nation did not sacrifice." Reported by Ahmad, Abu Dawud, and al-Tirmidhi.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Yazid ibn Abi Habib, from Ibn Abbas, from Jabir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ sacrificed two rams on the day of the festival, and when he turned them to face the direction, he said: "I have turned my face to Him who created the heavens and the earth, as one inclining truly to Allah, a Muslim, and I am not among the polytheists. Indeed my prayer, my rites of worship, my life and my death are for Allah, Lord of the worlds. He has no partner, and thus I have been commanded, and I am the first of the Muslims. O Allah, from You and to You, and on behalf of Muhammad and his nation." Then he mentioned the name of Allah, proclaimed His greatness, and slaughtered.

From Ali ibn al-Husayn, from Abu Rafi': that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, when he offered sacrifice, would buy two fat, horned, piebald rams. When he had prayed and delivered the sermon to the people, one of them would be brought to him while he was standing in his place of prayer, and he would slaughter it himself with the knife, then say: "O Allah, this is on behalf of my entire nation, whoever bears witness to You of Your Oneness and bears witness for me of the delivery of the message." Then the other would be brought and he would slaughter it himself, then say: "This is on behalf of Muhammad and the family of Muhammad." He would then feed both of them entirely to the poor, [and eat] himself and his family from them. Reported by Ahmad and Ibn Majah.

Al-A'mash said, from Abu Dhibyan, from Ibn Abbas, regarding His statement, {So mention the name of Allah over them, standing in rows}: he said, standing on three legs, with the left foreleg tied up, and one says: "In the name of Allah, and Allah is greatest. O Allah, from You and to You." Similarly it was reported by Mujahid, Ali ibn Abi Talhah, and al-Awfi, from Ibn Abbas, in like manner.

Layth said, from Mujahid: when its left leg is tied, it stands on three. Ibn Abi Najih reported similarly from him.

Al-Dahhak said: one leg is tied, so it stands on three.

In the two Sahihs, from Ibn Umar: that he came upon a man who had made his badanah kneel and was slaughtering it while it was in that position, and he said: "Raise it up standing, with its leg tied, the way of the Father of al-Qasim ﷺ."

From Jabir: that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and his companions used to slaughter the budn with the left foreleg tied, standing on the remaining legs. Reported by Abu Dawud.

Ibn Lahi'ah said: Ata' ibn Dinar told me that Salim ibn Abdullah said to Sulayman ibn Abd al-Malik: "Stand on its right side, and slaughter from its left side."

In Sahih Muslim, from Jabir, in the description of the Farewell Pilgrimage, he said therein: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ slaughtered with his own hand sixty-three camels, thrusting a spear that was in his hand into them.

Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar informed us, from Qatadah, who said: in the reading of Ibn Mas'ud it is "sawafin," meaning tied up while standing.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Mansur, from Mujahid: whoever reads it "sawafin" means tied up, and whoever reads it {sawaff} means arranged in rows before it.

Tawus, al-Hasan, and others said: "So mention the name of Allah over them, sawafi," meaning: exclusively devoted to Allah, Mighty and Majestic. This was likewise reported by Malik, from al-Zuhri.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd said: "sawafi" means there is no partnership in them like the partnership of the pre-Islamic era in their idols.

Regarding His statement, {and when their sides have fallen}: Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid: meaning, they have fallen to the ground.

This is also a report from Ibn Abbas, and Muqatil ibn Hayyan said likewise.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: {and when their sides have fallen} means: it has been slaughtered.

Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd ibn Aslam said: {and when their sides have fallen} means: it has died.

This last view is what Ibn Abbas and Mujahid intended, for it is not permissible to eat from the badanah once slaughtered until it dies and its movement has grown cold. It has come in a marfu' (elevated) hadith: "Do not hasten the souls to depart." This was reported by al-Thawri in his Jami', from Ayyub, from Yahya ibn Abi Kathir, from Farafisah al-Hanafi, from Umar ibn al-Khattab, that he said this. It is supported by the hadith of Shaddad ibn Aws in Sahih Muslim: "Indeed Allah has decreed excellence in all things. So when you kill, kill well, and when you slaughter, slaughter well. Let each of you sharpen his blade and let him put his slaughtered animal at ease."

From Abu Waqid al-Laythi, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whatever is cut off from an animal while it is still alive is dead flesh (carrion)." Reported by Ahmad, Abu Dawud, and al-Tirmidhi, who deemed it authentic.

Regarding His statement, {So eat of them and feed the qani' (contented poor) and the mu'tarr (one who presents himself)}: some of the predecessors said: His statement {So eat of them} is a command of permission.

Malik said: this is recommended. Others said: it is obligatory. This is one view among some of the Shafi'is. They differed over the intended meaning of al-qani' and al-mu'tarr. Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: al-qani' is the one who is content with what you give him, remaining in his home. Al-mu'tarr is the one who presents himself to you and comes to you so that you might give him some of the meat, without asking. Mujahid and Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi said likewise.

Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: al-qani' is the one who abstains from asking, and al-mu'tarr is the one who asks. This is the view of Qatadah, Ibrahim al-Nakha'i, and Mujahid in one report from him.

Ibn Abbas, Zayd ibn Aslam, Ikrimah, al-Hasan al-Basri, Ibn al-Kalbi, Muqatil ibn Hayyan, and Malik ibn Anas said: al-qani' is the one who comes humbly to you and asks you, and al-mu'tarr is the one who presents himself to you, showing his need without asking you. This is the wording of al-Hasan.

Sa'id ibn Jubayr said: al-qani' is the one who asks, then he said: Have you not heard the saying of al-Shammakh: "Indeed a man's wealth sets him right and frees him from his poverty, more chaste than qunu'." He said: meaning, than asking. Ibn Zayd said the same.

Zayd ibn Aslam said: al-qani' is the poor person who goes around asking, and al-mu'tarr is the friend and the weak person who comes to visit. This is also a report from Abdullah ibn Zayd.

From Mujahid also: al-qani' is your wealthy neighbor [who observes what enters your house], and al-mu'tarr is the one among the people who presents himself to you.

And from him: that al-qani' (the contented one) is the one who covets (i.e., asks with hope). And al-mu'tarr is the one who presents himself near the sacrificial animals, whether rich or poor.

And from Ikrimah similarly. And from him: al-qani' means the people of Makkah.

Ibn Jarir chose the view that al-qani' is the one who asks (the beggar), because it derives from "aqna'a" with his hand, when he raises it to ask. And al-mu'tarr is from al-i'tirar, which is: the one who presents himself for the eating of the meat.

Some scholars used this noble verse as evidence that the sacrificial animal (udhiyyah) should be divided into three portions: a third for its owner to eat from, a third to give as a gift to his companions, and a third to give in charity to the poor, because Allah, exalted is He, said: {So eat of it and feed the qani' and the mu'tarr}. And in the authentic hadith, the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to the people: "I had forbidden you from storing the meat of the sacrifices beyond three days, but now eat and store as much as seems good to you." And in another narration: "so eat, store, and give in charity." And in another narration: "so eat, feed others, and give in charity."

The second view is that the one offering the sacrifice eats half and gives half in charity, based on His saying in the aforementioned verse: {So eat of it and feed the miserable poor one} [al-Hajj: 28], and based on his saying in the hadith: "so eat, store, and give in charity."

If he eats all of it, it was said: he owes no compensation for anything. This is the view of Ibn Surayj among the Shafi'is.

Some of them said: he must compensate for all of it, either with its like or its value. And it was said: he must compensate for half of it. And it was said: a third of it. And it was said: the smallest portion of it. This is the well-known position within the Shafi'i school.

As for the hides, in the Musnad of Ahmad, from Qatadah ibn al-Nu'man, in the hadith concerning the sacrifices: "so eat, give in charity, make use of their hides, and do not sell them."

Among the scholars there are those who permitted that, and among them there are those who said: he should share the price of it with the poor. And Allah knows best.

[A matter of discussion]

From al-Bara' ibn Azib, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The first thing we begin with on this day of ours is that we pray, then we return and slaughter. Whoever does that has attained our sunnah, and whoever slaughters before the prayer, it is merely meat he has hastened for his family; it counts for nothing of the sacred rite." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it.

For this reason al-Shafi'i and a group of scholars said: the beginning of the time for the sacrifice (al-adha) is when the sun rises on the Day of Sacrifice and the time of the Eid prayer and the two sermons has elapsed. Ahmad added: and that the imam should slaughter after that, because of what came in Sahih Muslim: "and that you should not slaughter until the imam has slaughtered."

Abu Hanifah said: as for the people of the countryside villages and similar places, they may slaughter after the break of dawn, since in his view there is no Eid prayer prescribed for them. As for the people of the cities, they should not slaughter until the imam has prayed. And Allah knows best.

Then it was said: slaughtering is only prescribed on the Day of Sacrifice alone. And it was said: the Day of Sacrifice applies to the people of the cities, because sacrificial animals are readily available to them, while for the people of the villages it is the Day of Sacrifice and the Days of Tashriq (the days of drying meat) that follow it. This is the view of Sa'id ibn Jubayr. And it was said: the Day of Sacrifice and one day after it, for everyone. And it was said: and two days after it, and this is the view of Ahmad. And it was said: the Day of Sacrifice and the three Days of Tashriq after it, and this is the view of al-Shafi'i, based on the hadith of Jubayr ibn Mut'im, that the Messenger of Allah, may Allah bless him and grant him peace, said: "And the days of Tashriq are all days for slaughtering." Narrated by Ahmad and Ibn Hibban.

And it was said: that the time for slaughtering extends to the end of Dhu al-Hijjah, and this is the view of Ibrahim al-Nakha'i and Abu Salamah ibn Abd al-Rahman. And it is a gharib (unusual, singular) view.

And His saying: {Thus have We subjected them to you, that you may be grateful}: Allah, exalted is He, says: for this reason {We subjected them to you}, meaning: We made them tractable for you, meaning: We made them submissive and compliant to you. If you wish, you ride them, and if you wish, you milk them, and if you wish, you slaughter them, just as Allah, exalted is He, said: {Have they not seen that We have created for them, among the things Our hands have made, cattle, which they possess? And We have made them tractable for them, so that some of them they ride and some of them they eat. And they have in them benefits and drinks. Will they not then be grateful?} [Ya-Sin: 71-73]. And He said in this noble verse: {Thus have We subjected them to you, that you may be grateful}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُمْتَنًّا عَلَى عِبَادِهِ فِيمَا خَلَقَ لَهُمْ مِنَ الْبُدْنِ، وَجَعَلَهَا مِنْ شَعَائِرِهِ، وَهُوَ أَنَّهُ جَعَلَهَا تُهْدَى إِلَى بَيْتِهِ الْحَرَامِ، بَلْ هِيَ أَفْضَلُ مَا يُهْدَى [إِلَى بَيْتِهِ الْحَرَامِ] ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿لَا تُحِلُّوا شَعَائِرَ اللَّهِ وَلا الشَّهْرَ الْحَرَامَ وَلا الْهَدْيَ وَلا الْقَلائِدَ [وَلا آمِّينَ الْبَيْتَ الْحَرَامَ يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلا مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ وَرِضْوَانًا] ﴾ الْآيَةَ: [الْمَائِدَةِ: ٢] .

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيج: قَالَ عَطَاءٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالْبُدْنَ جَعَلْنَاهَا لَكُمْ مِنْ شَعَائِرِ اللَّهِ﴾ ، قَالَ: الْبَقَرَةُ، وَالْبَعِيرُ. وَكَذَا رُوي عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، وَالْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ. وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: إِنَّمَا الْبُدْنُ مِنَ الْإِبِلِ.

قُلْتُ: أَمَّا إِطْلَاقُ البَدَنة عَلَى الْبَعِيرِ فَمُتَّفَقٌ عَلَيْهِ، وَاخْتَلَفُوا فِي صِحَّةِ إِطْلَاقِ الْبَدَنَةِ عَلَى الْبَقَرَةِ، عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ، أَصَحُّهُمَا أَنَّهُ يُطْلَقُ عَلَيْهَا ذَلِكَ شَرْعًا كَمَا صَحَّ فِي الْحَدِيثِ.

ثُمَّ جُمْهُورُ الْعُلَمَاءِ عَلَى أَنَّهُ تُجزئ الْبَدَنَةُ عَنْ سَبْعَةٍ، وَالْبَقَرَةُ عَنْ سَبْعَةٍ، كَمَا ثَبَتَ بِهِ الْحَدِيثُ عِنْدَ مُسْلِمٍ، مِنْ رِوَايَةِ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ [وَغَيْرِهِ] ، قَالَ: أَمَرَنَا رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إن نشتركَ في الأضاحي، البدنةُ عَنْ سَبْعَةٍ، وَالْبَقَرَةُ عَنْ سَبْعَةٍ .

[وَقَالَ إسحاق بنُ رَاهَويه وَغَيْرُهُ: بَلْ تُجزئ الْبَقَرَةُ عَنْ سَبْعَةٍ، وَالْبَعِيرُ عَنْ عَشَرَةٍ] . وَقَدْ وَرَدَ بِهِ حَدِيثٌ فِي مُسْنَدِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، وَسُنَنِ النَّسَائِيِّ، وَغَيْرِهِمَا ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا خَيْرٌ﴾ ، أَيْ: ثَوَابٌ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ.

وَعَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ يَزِيدَ الْكَعْبِيِّ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ عُرْوَة، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا عَمِل ابْنُ آدَمَ يَوْمَ النَّحْرِ عَمَلًا أَحَبَّ إِلَى اللَّهِ مِنْ هِرَاقه دَمٍ، وَإِنَّهُ لَتَأْتِي يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ بِقُرُونِهَا وَأَظْلَافِهَا وَأَشْعَارِهَا، وَإِنَّ الدَّمَ لَيَقَعُ مِنَ اللَّهِ بِمَكَانٍ، قَبْلَ أَنْ يَقَعَ عَلَى الْأَرْضِ، فطِيبُوا بِهَا نَفْسًا". رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ وحَسنه .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ: كَانَ أَبُو حَاتِمٍ يَسْتَدِينُ وَيَسُوقُ البُدْن، فَقِيلَ لَهُ: تَسْتَدِينُ وَتَسُوقُ الْبُدْنَ؟ فَقَالَ: إِنِّي سَمِعْتُ اللَّهَ يَقُولُ: ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا خَيْرٌ﴾

وَعَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى الله عليه وسلم: "ما أُنْفِقَتِ الوَرقَ فِي شَيْءٍ أفضلَ مِنْ نَحِيرَةٍ فِي يَوْمِ عِيدٍ". رَوَاهُ الدَّارَقُطْنِيُّ فِي سُنَنِهِ .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: ﴿لَكُمْ فِيهَا خَيْرٌ﴾ قَالَ: أَجْرٌ وَمَنَافِعُ.

وَقَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيّ: يَرْكَبُهَا وَيَحْلِبُهَا إِذَا احْتَاجَ إِلَيْهَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَاذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا صَوَافَّ﴾ وَعَنِ [الْمُطَّلِبِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ حَنْطَبٍ، عَنْ] جابر ابن عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: صليتُ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ عيدَ الْأَضْحَى، فَلَمَّا انصَرَفَ أَتَى بِكَبْشٍ فَذَبَحَهُ، فَقَالَ: "بِسْمِ اللَّهِ وَاللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ، اللَّهُمَّ هَذَا عَنِّي وَعَمَّنْ لَمَّ يُضَحِّ مِنْ أُمَّتِي".

رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ .

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: ضَحَّى رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِكَبْشَيْنِ فِي يَوْمِ عِيدٍ، فَقَالَ حين وجههما: "وجهت وجهي للذي فطر السموات وَالْأَرْضَ حَنِيفًا مُسْلِمًا، وَمَا أَنَا مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ، إِنَّ صَلَاتِي وَنُسُكِي وَمَحْيَايَ وَمَمَاتِي لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ. لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَبِذَلِكَ أُمِرْتُ، وَأَنَا أَوَّلُ الْمُسْلِمِينَ، اللَّهُمَّ مِنْكَ وَلَكَ، وَعَنْ مُحَمَّدٍ وأمته". ثم سمى الله وكبر وَذَبَحَ .

وَعَنْ عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، عَنْ أَبِي رَافِعٍ؛ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ إِذَا ضَحَّى اشْتَرَى كَبْشَيْنِ سَمِينَيْنِ أَقْرَنَيْنِ أَمْلَحَيْنِ، فَإِذَا صَلَّى وَخَطَبَ النَّاسَ أُتِيَ بِأَحَدِهِمَا وَهُوَ قَائِمٌ فِي مُصَلَّاهُ فَذَبَحَهُ بِنَفْسِهِ بِالْمُدْيَةِ ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: "اللَّهُمَّ هَذَا عَنْ أُمَّتِي جَمِيعِهَا، مَنْ شَهِدَ لَكَ بِالتَّوْحِيدِ وَشَهِدَ لِي بِالْبَلَاغِ". ثُمَّ يُؤتى بِالْآخَرِ فَيَذْبَحُهُ بِنَفْسِهِ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُ: "هَذَا عَنْ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ" فيُطعمها جَمِيعًا الْمَسَاكِينَ، [وَيَأْكُلُ] هُوَ وَأَهْلُهُ مِنْهُمَا.

رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ .

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ أَبِي ظِبْيَان، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَاذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا صَوَافَّ﴾ ، قَالَ: قِيَامٌ عَلَى ثَلَاثِ قَوَائِمَ، مَعْقُولَةٌ يدُها الْيُسْرَى، يَقُولُ: "بِسْمِ اللَّهِ وَاللَّهُ أَكْبَرُ ، اللَّهُمَّ مِنْكَ وَلَكَ". وَكَذَلِكَ رَوَى مُجَاهِدٌ، وَعَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، والعَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، نَحْوَ هَذَا.

وَقَالَ لَيْثٌ. عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: إِذَا عُقلت رِجْلُهَا الْيُسْرَى قَامَتْ عَلَى ثَلَاثٍ. ورَوَى ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْهُ، نَحْوَهُ .

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: تُعقل رِجْلٌ وَاحِدَةٌ فَتَكُونُ عَلَى ثَلَاثٍ.

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنِ ابْنِ عُمَرَ: أَنَّهُ أَتَى عَلَى رَجُلٍ قَدْ أَنَاخَ بَدَنته وَهُوَ يَنْحَرُهَا، فَقَالَ: ابْعَثْهَا قِيَامًا مُقَيَّدَةً سُنَّةُ أَبِي الْقَاسِمِ ﷺ .

وَعَنْ جَابِرٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ وأصحابَه كَانُوا ينحَرون البُدْن معقولةَ الْيُسْرَى، قَائِمَةً عَلَى مَا بَقِيَ مِنْ قَوَائِمِهَا. رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ .

وَقَالَ ابْنُ لَهِيعة: حَدَّثَنِي عَطَاءُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ، أَنَّ سَالِمَ بْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ لِسُلَيْمَانَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ: قفْ مِنْ شِقِّهَا الْأَيْمَنِ، وانْحَر مِنْ شِقِّهَا الْأَيْسَرِ.

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ، فِي صِفَةِ حِجَّةِ الوَدَاع، قَالَ فِيهِ: فَنَحَرَ رسولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِيَدِهِ ثَلَاثًا وَسِتِّينَ بَدَنة، جَعَلَ يَطعَنُها بحَربة فِي يَدِهِ .

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَر، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ قَالَ: فِي حَرْفِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: "صَوَافِنَ"، أَيْ: مُعقَّلة قِيَامًا .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: مَن قَرَأَهَا "صَوَافِنَ" قَالَ: مَعْقُولَةٌ. وَمَنْ قَرَأَهَا ﴿صَوَافَّ﴾ قَالَ: تُصَفُّ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهَا.

وَقَالَ طَاوُسٌ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا: "فَاذْكُرُوا اسْمَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْهَا صَوَافِيَ" يَعْنِي: خَالِصَةً لِلَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ. وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مَالِكٌ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدٍ: "صوافيَ": لَيْسَ فِيهَا شِرْكٌ كَشِرْكِ الْجَاهِلِيَّةِ لِأَصْنَامِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَإِذَا وَجَبَتْ جُنُوبُهَا﴾ قَالَ: ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: يَعْنِي: سَقَطَتْ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ.

وَهُوَ رِوَايَةٌ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَكَذَا قَالَ مُقَاتِلُ بْنُ حَيَّانَ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَإِذَا وَجَبَتْ جُنُوبُهَا﴾ يَعْنِي: نُحِرَتْ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ: ﴿فَإِذَا وَجَبَتْ جُنُوبُهَا﴾ يَعْنِي: مَاتَتْ.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ هُوَ مُرَادُ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ وَمُجَاهِدٍ، فَإِنَّهُ لَا يَجُوزُ الْأَكْلُ مِنَ البَدَنة إِذَا نُحرت حَتَّى تَمُوتَ وتَبْرد حَرَكَتُهَا. وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي حَدِيثٍ مَرْفُوعٍ: "وَلَا تُعجِلُوا النفوسَ أَنْ تَزْهَق" . وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ الثَّوْرِيُّ فِي جَامِعِهِ، عَنْ أَيُّوبَ، عَنْ يَحْيَى ابْنِ أَبِي كَثِيرٍ، عَنْ فَرافصَة الْحَنَفِيِّ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ الْخَطَّابِ؛ أَنَّهُ قَالَ ذَلِكَ وَيُؤَيِّدُهُ حَدِيثُ شَدّاد بْنِ أَوْسٍ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَتَبَ الْإِحْسَانَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ، فَإِذَا قَتَلْتُمْ فَأَحْسِنُوا القِتْلة، وَإِذَا ذَبَحْتُمْ فَأَحْسِنُوا الذَّبْحَ ولْيُحدَّ أَحَدُكُمْ شَفْرَته، ولْيُرِحْ ذَبِيحته" .

وَعَنْ أَبِي وَاقِدٍ اللَّيْثِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَا قُطع مِنَ الْبَهِيمَةِ وَهِيَ حَيَّةٌ، فَهُوَ مَيْتَةٌ".

رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ وَصَحَّحَهُ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا وَأَطْعِمُوا الْقَانِعَ وَالْمُعْتَرَّ َ﴾ قَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ : قَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا﴾ أَمْرُ إِبَاحَةٍ.

وَقَالَ مَالِكٌ: يُسْتَحَبُّ ذَلِكَ. وَقَالَ غَيْرُهُ: يَجِبُ. وَهُوَ وَجْه لِبَعْضِ الشَّافِعِيَّةِ. وَاخْتُلِفَ فِي الْمُرَادِ بِالْقَانِعِ وَالْمُعْتَرِّ، فَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْقَانِعُ: الْمُسْتَغْنِي بِمَا أَعْطَيْتَهُ، وَهُوَ فِي بَيْتِهِ. وَالْمُعْتَرُّ: الَّذِي يَتَعَرَّضُ لَكَ، ويُلمّ بِكَ أَنْ تُعْطِيَهُ مِنَ اللَّحْمِ، وَلَا يَسْأَلُ. وَكَذَا قال مجاهد، ومحمد بن كعب القُرَظِيّ.

وَقَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: الْقَانِعُ: الْمُتَعَفِّفُ. وَالْمُعْتَرُّ: السَّائِلُ. وَهَذَا قولُ قَتَادَةَ، وَإِبْرَاهِيمَ النَّخَعي، وَمُجَاهِدٍ فِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَزَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ وعِكْرِمَة ، وَالْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ، وَابْنُ الْكَلْبِيِّ، ومُقَاتِل بْنُ حَيَّان، وَمَالِكُ بْنُ أَنَسٍ: الْقَانِعُ: هُوَ الَّذِي يَقْنع إِلَيْكَ وَيَسْأَلُكَ. وَالْمُعْتَرُّ: الَّذِي يَعْتَرِيكَ، يَتَضَرَّعُ وَلَا يَسْأَلُكَ. وَهَذَا لَفْظُ الْحَسَنِ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ: الْقَانِعُ: هُوَ السَّائِلُ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: أَمَا سَمِعْتَ قَوْلَ الشَّمَّاخ. لَمَالُ المَرْءِ يُصْلِحُه فَيُغْني ... مَفَاقِرَه ، أَعَفُّ مِنَ القُنُوع 

قَالَ: يَعْنِي مِنَ السُّؤَّالِ، وَبِهِ قَالَ ابْنُ زَيْدٍ.

وَقَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ أَسْلَمَ: الْقَانِعُ: الْمِسْكِينُ الَّذِي يَطُوفُ. وَالْمُعْتَرُّ: الصَّدِيقُ وَالضَّعِيفُ الَّذِي يَزُورُ. وَهُوَ رِوَايَةٌ عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ أَيْضًا.

وَعَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ أَيْضًا: الْقَانِعُ: جَارُكَ الْغَنِيُّ [الَّذِي يُبْصِرُ مَا يَدْخُلُ بَيْتَكَ] وَالْمُعْتَرُّ: الَّذِي يَعْتَرِيكَ مِنَ النَّاسِ.

وَعَنْهُ: أَنَّ الْقَانِعَ: هُوَ الطَّامِعُ. وَالْمُعْتَرُّ: هُوَ الَّذِي يَعْتَر بالبُدْن مِنْ غَنِيٍّ أَوْ فَقِيرٍ.

وَعَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ نَحْوُهُ، وَعَنْهُ الْقَانِعُ: أَهْلُ مَكَّةَ.

وَاخْتَارَ ابنُ جَرِيرٍ أَنَّ الْقَانِعَ: هُوَ السَّائِلُ؛ لِأَنَّهُ مَنْ أَقْنَعَ بِيَدِهِ إِذَا رَفَعَهَا لِلسُّؤَالِ، وَالْمُعْتَرُّ مِنَ الِاعْتِرَارِ، وَهُوَ: الَّذِي يَتَعَرَّضُ لِأَكْلِ اللَّحْمِ.

وَقَدِ احْتَجَّ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ مَن ذَهَبَ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ إِلَى أَنَّ الْأُضْحِيَّةُ تُجزَّأ ثَلَاثَةَ أَجْزَاءٍ: فَثُلُثٌ لِصَاحِبِهَا يَأْكُلُهُ [مِنْهَا] ، وَثُلُثٌ يُهْدِيهِ لِأَصْحَابِهِ، وَثُلُثٌ يَتَصَدَّقُ بِهِ عَلَى الْفُقَرَاءِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ تَعَالَى قَالَ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا وَأَطْعِمُوا الْقَانِعَ وَالْمُعْتَرَّ﴾ . وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ لِلنَّاسِ: "إِنِّي كُنْتُ نَهَيْتُكُمْ عَنِ ادِّخَارِ لُحُومِ الْأَضَاحِيِّ فَوْقَ ثَلَاثٍ، فَكَلُّوا وَادَّخِرُوا مَا بَدَا لَكُمْ" وَفِي رواية: "فكلوا وادخروا وتصدقوا". وفي رواية: "فكلوا وأطعموا وتصدقوا" .

وَالْقَوْلُ الثَّانِي: إِنَّ الْمُضَحِّيَ يَأْكُلُ النِّصْفَ وَيَتَصَدَّقُ بِالنِّصْفِ، لِقَوْلِهِ فِي الْآيَةِ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ: ﴿فَكُلُوا مِنْهَا وَأَطْعِمُوا الْبَائِسَ الْفَقِيرَ﴾ [الْحَجِّ: ٢٨] ، وَلِقَوْلِهِ فِي الْحَدِيثِ: "فَكُلُوا وَادَّخِرُوا وَتَصَدَّقُوا".

فَإِنْ أَكَلَ الْكُلَّ فَقِيلَ : لَا يُضَمِّنُ شَيْئًا. وَبِهِ قَالَ ابْنُ سُرَيج من الشافعية.

وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: يُضَمِّنُهَا كُلَّهَا بِمِثْلِهَا أَوْ قِيمَتِهَا. وَقِيلَ: يُضَمِّنُ نِصْفَهَا. وَقِيلَ: ثُلُثَهَا. وَقِيلَ: أَدْنَى جُزْءٍ مِنْهَا. وَهُوَ الْمَشْهُورُ مِنْ مَذْهَبِ الشَّافِعِيِّ.

وَأَمَّا الْجُلُودُ، فَفِي مُسْنَدِ أَحْمَدَ عَنْ قَتَادَةَ ابن النُّعْمَانِ فِي حَدِيثِ الْأَضَاحِيِّ: "فَكُلُوا وَتَصَّدَّقُوا، وَاسْتَمْتِعُوا بِجُلُودِهَا، وَلَا تَبِيعُوهَا" .

وَمِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ مَنْ رَخَّصَ [فِي ذَلِكَ] ، وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ قَالَ: يُقَاسِمُ الْفُقَرَاءَ ثَمَنَهَا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

[مَسْأَلَةٌ] .

عَنِ الْبَرَاءِ بْنِ عَازِبٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَوَّلَ مَا نَبْدَأُ بِهِ فِي يَوْمِنَا هَذَا أَنْ نُصَلِّيَ، ثُمَّ نَرْجِعَ فَنَنْحَرَ. فَمَنْ فَعَلَ ذَلِكَ فَقَدْ أَصَابَ سُنَّتَنَا، وَمَنْ ذَبَحَ قَبْلَ الصَّلَاةِ فَإِنَّمَا هُوَ لَحْمٌ [عَجَّلَهُ] لِأَهْلِهِ، لَيْسَ مِنَ النُّسُكِ فِي شَيْءٍ" أَخْرَجَاهُ .

فَلِهَذَا قَالَ الشَّافِعِيُّ وَجَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ الْعُلَمَاءِ: إِنَّ أَوَّلَ وَقْتِ الْأَضْحَى إِذَا طَلَعَتِ الشَّمْسُ يَوْمَ النَّحْرِ، وَمَضَى قَدْرُ صَلَاةِ الْعِيدِ وَالْخُطْبَتَيْنِ. زَادَ أَحْمَدُ: وَأَنْ يَذْبَحَ الْإِمَامُ بَعْدَ ذَلِكَ، لِمَا جَاءَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ: وَأَلَّا تَذْبَحُوا حَتَّى يَذْبَحَ الْإِمَامُ" .

وَقَالَ أَبُو حَنِيفَةَ: أَمَّا أَهْلُ السَّوَادِ مِنَ الْقُرَى وَنَحْوِهِمْ ، فَلَهُمْ أَنْ يَذْبَحُوا بَعْدَ طُلُوعِ الْفَجْرِ، إِذْ لَا صَلَاةَ عِيدٍ عِنْدَهُ لَهُمْ. وَأَمَّا أَهْلُ الْأَمْصَارِ فَلَا يَذْبَحُوا حَتَّى يُصَلِّيَ الْإِمَامُ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

ثُمَّ قِيلَ: لَا يُشْرَعُ الذَّبْحُ إِلَّا يَوْمَ النَّحْرِ وَحْدَهُ. وَقِيلَ: يَوْمُ النَّحْرِ لِأَهْلِ الْأَمْصَارِ، لِتَيَسُّرِ الْأَضَاحِيِّ عِنْدَهُمْ، وَأَمَّا أَهْلُ الْقُرَى فَيَوْمُ النَّحْرِ وَأَيَّامُ التَّشْرِيقِ بَعْدَهُ، وَبِهِ قَالَ سَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ. وَقِيلَ: يَوْمُ النَّحْرِ، وَيَوْمٌ بَعْدَهُ لِلْجَمِيعِ. وَقِيلَ: وَيَوْمَانِ بَعْدَهُ، وَبِهِ قَالَ أَحْمَدُ. وَقِيلَ: يَوْمُ النَّحْرِ وَثَلَاثَةُ أَيَّامِ التَّشْرِيقِ بَعْدَهُ، وَبِهِ قَالَ الشَّافِعِيُّ؛ لِحَدِيثِ جُبَيْرِ بْنِ مُطْعِمٍ: أَنَّ رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم قال: "وَأَيَّامُ التَّشْرِيقِ كُلُّهَا ذَبْحٌ". رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ وَابْنُ حِبَّانَ .

وَقِيلَ: إِنَّ وَقْتَ الذَّبْحِ يَمْتَدُّ إِلَى آخَرِ ذِي الْحِجَّةِ، وَبِهِ قَالَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ النَّخَعِيّ، وَأَبُو سَلَمَةَ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ. وَهُوَ قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ سَخَّرْنَاهَا لَكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ﴾ : يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: مِنْ أَجْلِ هَذَا ﴿سَخَّرْنَاهَا لَكُم﴾ أَيْ: ذَلَّلْنَاهَا لَكُمْ، أَيْ: جَعَلْنَاهَا مُنْقَادَةً لَكُمْ خَاضِعَةً، إِنْ شِئْتُمْ رَكِبْتُمْ، وَإِنْ شِئْتُمْ حَلَبْتُمْ، وَإِنْ شِئْتُمْ ذَبَحْتُمْ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَوْا أَنَّا خَلَقْنَا لَهُمْ مِمَّا عَمِلَتْ أَيْدِينَا أَنْعَامًا فَهُمْ لَهَا مَالِكُونَ. وَذَلَّلْنَاهَا لَهُمْ فَمِنْهَا رَكُوبُهُمْ وَمِنْهَا يَأْكُلُونَ. وَلَهُمْ فِيهَا مَنَافِعُ وَمَشَارِبُ أَفَلا يَشْكُرُونَ﴾ [يس: ٧١ -٧٣] ، وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿كَذَلِكَ سَخَّرْنَاهَا لَكُمْ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ﴾

---

## 22:37 — verse 37

### Translation

The Almighty says: He has only prescribed for you the slaughtering of these sacrificial animals and offerings so that you may remember Him when slaughtering them, for He is the Creator, the Provider, and it is not that anything of their flesh or blood reaches Him. He, the Exalted, is Self-Sufficient, free of need of anything besides Himself.

In their pre-Islamic ignorance, when they slaughtered animals for their gods, they used to place some of the flesh of their sacrifices upon them and sprinkle some of their blood upon them. So the Almighty said: {The flesh of them will not reach Allah, nor will their blood}

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Ibn Jurayj said: the people of pre-Islamic ignorance used to sprinkle the House (the Ka'bah) with the flesh and blood of camels. The companions of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "We are more entitled to sprinkle it." So Allah revealed: {The flesh of them will not reach Allah, nor will their blood, but what reaches Him is your piety}, meaning: He accepts that and rewards for it.

As it is stated in the authentic hadith: "Indeed Allah does not look at your outward forms nor at your wealth, but He looks at your hearts and your deeds." And as it is stated in the hadith: "Indeed charity falls into the hand of the Merciful before it falls into the hand of the one who asks, and indeed blood falls with Allah in a place before it falls upon the earth," as the hadith mentioned previously. It was narrated by Ibn Majah and al-Tirmidhi, who deemed it hasan (sound), from Aishah as a raised report (marfu'). Its meaning is that it was conveyed to establish the reality of acceptance from Allah for one who is sincere in his deed, and it has no meaning that comes to mind among the verifying scholars other than this. And Allah knows best.

Waki' said, from [Yahya] ibn Muslim Abu al-Dahhak: I asked 'Amir al-Sha'bi about the hides of sacrificial animals, and he said: {The flesh of them will not reach Allah, nor will their blood}. If you wish, sell them; if you wish, keep them; and if you wish, give them in charity.

His saying: {Thus have We subjected them to you} means: for this reason He subjected the sacrificial camels to you, {so that you may glorify Allah for having guided you}, meaning: so that you may exalt Him as He has guided you to His religion and His law and to what He loves and what pleases Him, and has forbidden you from doing what He dislikes and rejects.

His saying: {And give glad tidings to the doers of good} means: give glad tidings, O Muhammad, to the doers of good, that is, in their deeds, those who uphold the limits set by Allah, who follow what He has prescribed for them, who believe the Messenger regarding what he conveyed to them and brought to them from his Lord, Mighty and Majestic is He.

[A matter of jurisprudence]

Abu Hanifah, Malik, and al-Thawri held the view that the sacrifice (udhiyyah) is obligatory upon one who possesses the minimum threshold of wealth (nisab), and Abu Hanifah added the condition of being a resident (not a traveler) as well. They argued for this using what Ahmad and Ibn Majah narrated with a chain whose men are all trustworthy, from Abu Hurayrah as a raised report: "Whoever finds himself with the means and does not offer a sacrifice, let him not approach our place of prayer." However, this hadith contains an element of being gharib (singular/unusual), and Ahmad ibn Hanbal considered it objectionable.

Ibn 'Umar said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ remained ten years offering sacrifices. Narrated by al-Tirmidhi.

Al-Shafi'i and Ahmad said: the sacrifice is not obligatory, rather it is recommended, based on what is stated in the hadith: "There is no due right upon wealth besides zakat." It has already been mentioned that he, peace be upon him, sacrificed on behalf of his nation, and that this removed the obligation of it from them.

Abu Sarihah said: I was a neighbor of Abu Bakr and 'Umar, and they would not offer sacrifices for fear that people would imitate them.
